O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	O you, very dear son, I have completed this book that is the essence of medical knowledge together with its fulfillment, and I have finished it through its explanations and declarations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	And it came to me in a vision that I would complete this treatise with you, which is part of the work by hand, that is to say "surgery".
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	And because the work by hand is practiced in our region and spread throughout everywhere, it is excellent in science and capability, and is not delayed from its force but only the small descriptions in books of the ancients that hands have moved.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	And because of this, there has come error and vanity, and intentions are closed up, and science is removed.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation;	Or me seems that I will vivify it together with the order of this physician according to the way of exposure and declaration and of the abbreviation;
et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	And I will come together with the forms of the caustic tools, and of the other instruments of the work, with the setting of the declaration and preparation of it, as is fitting.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	And for this reason, because there are no good hands masters found in our time, is the art of medicine extended.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	And he who deals with it must master the science of anatomy, as Galen says, as far as he knows the shape and arrangement and separation of the organs, and has knowledge of bones and nerves and veins and the number of bones, and the movement and flowing veins and resting veins, and their source.
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc;	And for this dist Icopra that it does not hurt with the non-existence, and hurts with the work a little.
et meismement en l’art de main.	and mainly in the art of hands.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes;	We tell you in the introduction to this book that he who is not knowledgeable about the things previously said should guard himself so that he does not make a mistake and harm men.
ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	before I have wanted many times of these who meddle in this science, and if they abandon themselves to this science and to no experience.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col;	I saw a foolish man who cut an abscess on the neck of a woman, and he cut the arteries at the base of the neck.
por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	because so much blood came out that the woman died in his hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans;	And I saw another foolish man who treated a stone in a man's neck, and the stone was large;
si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	he brought out with it a piece of the bladder, and the man died within three days.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	And I have also been called to treat it with a lever, and I saw the condition of the patient and the size of the stone; and if he treated it properly, he would not die.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie;	And I saw another foolish man who took in care an earl of our land who had a broken leg, and with the break there was a wound;
et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine;	and the foolish healer bound up the break over the wound with a tight bandage, and left no salve on the wound, and so he left it; and thus he finished.
et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie;	and he ordered that he not remove it;
et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	And it delays so that the leg was all stretched and the foot and came to perdition.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe;	I was called to come to him, and I hurried to come to undress the leg;
et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	and when I undid it so was at peace and did not feel any pain.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner;	But all ways corruption had already been confirmed on that member, and he could not heal it;
et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	and the corruption did not cease to spread through the member as long as the members were completely lost.
Et vis I autre mire qui effondra I apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	And I saw another miracle, that is, an abscess that was putrefied and then inflamed by the evil of its own nature.
Car chancre, quant il est purs d’umor melancolique, ne covient mie qu’on i(l) touche de fer s’il n’est en teil leu c’on puisse toute oster ce que est corrumpus.	For chalc, when it is purred with melancholic humor, will not come to touch it unless it is in a favorable position where one can completely remove what is corrupted.
Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions:	And for this, dear children, you are required to know that the work of hands is divided into two divisions:
c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions;	which means, namely, that it has danger in many dispositions;
et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	and I will show in each of the books of this book where there is fear and danger.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos.	For you are required to keep them so that the evil eye cannot speak ill of you.
Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez;	If you take your weapons in harmony, and undertake your patients lightly but firmly, and make use of the better way, so that through the grace of God you come to salvation and are saved.
et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit;	and leave the probable illnesses of great suffering.
et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	and hold your weapons back from that which makes you doubtful, and have faith that you may come from this world to glory.
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens:	Galien wrote some of these admonitions:
«Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	Do not take up the care of a bad illness, lest you be called a foolish healer.
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	I have devised this treatise according to III chapters.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez;	The first chapters are about fire cauterizations and medicinal aqueous treatments, and the order of the limbs;
et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	and the forms of instruments, and the ironing of cauterization, and all that is necessary in the work.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses;	The second chapters are about sizing and drilling, and suction cups and wounds, and extraction of arrows, and similar things;
et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	and this is the order of the chapters and the forms of instruments.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses;	The third chapter is about restoring dislocations and torsions and similar things;
et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	and here are ordered the parts of a pig's foot, and the forms of instruments.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	Thus we remember the work; it is necessary that I give the quality of the aid and the harm of each color.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus;	I say that the qualities of help, and harm, are the most distant word and subtle science and secret answers;
et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu;	and many wise men would speak about it, and agree with what is said;
et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	and I am satisfied with few words, because I shorten the length.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions:	I say that cautery helps universally in all complexions or it has matter, except for two complexions:
c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	that is to say, a hot complexion with matter and a dry complexion without matter.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide;	In a hot and dry complexion together with matter, there is none that would say that cautery is not of great help;
et li autre dirent le contraire:	and the other said the opposite:
que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	that cautery does not help with the disease that comes from heat and thirst.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour;	For nature's fire is too hot, and should not be used to treat any disease caused by heat or thirst;
et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	and it says that those who say the opposite are wrong: cautery does great help for hot and dry diseases which come in men's bodies.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	For when you compare the body of the man and his moisture to the complexion of fire, you find the body cold.
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	And I agree with this word.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	For I have not found it once by experiment.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens;	And any road, should not interfere but those who have tested it themselves, and who know by long experience the action of the ointment of cauterisation, and the diversity of complexions in men, and their temperaments and causes of their diseases, and their responses and the space of time.
des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	For we have no fear of other complexions, either by cold or moist diseases.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	And all this should come together and agree with the fire cautery.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	And know, children, that fire cautery will help in healing if there are secretions and of greater good than medicinal fire cautery.
Car li feus est simples, et ne vient mie fuers que au membre qui est cuis, et ne nuit a autre membre se poc nom.	For fire is simple, and it comes only to the member that is cooked, and it does not harm another member in any way.
Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation;	The burning remedies come from one member to another in moving away, and bring to the member great pain and injury in healing.
et par aventure ocit lou malaide.	and so the disease occurs.
Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	Fire for its height and because of the goodness of its substance does not cause this, unless there is an excess.
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses;	And I have found it by experience and because of the length of service and study that I have put into this art, and it is based on the truth of things;
et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant;	and I apologize for the length of the speech, because it does not please me that I should reveal the secret of fire, which is hidden in the work, and the quality of the art, how it drives away diseases from the body, as the philosopher says in demonstrating;
or le recevez en vos pensees.	receive it in your thoughts.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	And know, son, that they should be made at certain times and be performed with prayer.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere;	And I say that cauterization is appropriate at all times, because the harmful things resulting from it are overcome by the aid of cauterization;
et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	and most often cauterization is for necessary and urgent pains that cannot be endured until the time that greater injuries do not come to the member.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire;	And I never thought, son of a bitch, like they do in fucking hell.
car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue;	For the disease that is cured by fire has no return.
et il le dient ensi;	and serve it thus:
mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	but it is not as they fuck, because cauterization is only a type of medicine that changes the appearance of the skin and dries up the fluids that cause pain, and its effectiveness depends on the swiftness of its application, on its virtue and prowess.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut;	And it is possible for the disease to return according to the patient's complexion and the location and effectiveness of the medicine.
et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie;	And these excesses are accumulated in him through the acquisition of meat and similar things, unless cauterization is administered at the right time or place, where there is an accumulation of excess fluid and moisture due to pain, and similar things, and the pain does not return.
mais ce avient poc.	but this did not happen.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir;	And many people do not know that fire cauterization is one of the last resorts of medicine, and it is clear;
mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	but they do not believe that cauterization is worth anything after medicine, but their intentions are wrong, and cauterization is the last resort of medicine for when we cannot administer any other way of treatment in any disease, so let us administer the cauterization, and it is worthwhile.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	Therefore, it is clear that cauterization is the bloodletting of medicine, not according to the intention of the foolish, but
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance;	The ancient ones said that gold cauterization tools are smoother than those made of iron, and they only mentioned the quality of gold and its high purity;
et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes;	and they said that the color of the cauterization does not cause irritation, but this is not true because I have tested it, and I found that it does in some people;
et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	and gold cauterization is worth more than iron, as they said.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez;	And wherever you heat the gold instrument, you are not as hot as it is when it is heated by the color of gold, and it is sometimes cooled.
et s’on le chaufe trop;	and if it is overheated.
si font au feu;	if it is burned.
et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	and thus enough impediment.
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	And for this we use fire cautery which we have prepared for our work.
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	Or you may order this chapter of the heart to be read just as soon as possible, so that the vision may be easier to find.
dou cautere olivaire	The olive oil cautery
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	The olive oil cautery is good for a moisture and cold on the skull, and because of many humors that descend from the head through the hair, and through the ears, and for many dreams and pain in the teeth and pain in the throat, and especially for all diseases that come from cold such as paralysis and lameness and apoplexy and similar illnesses.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir;	The form of this cautery is that the patient be purged by a solu
et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	and then rub the head of the patient.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis;	And then place it on a cross between your hands and put your hands over his neck;
aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz;	afterwards, place the root of your palm on the root of his nose between his two eyes;
et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	and then place your two fingers, if it bleeds a little, heat the fire that is called "oliver," of which this form is:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant;	And put on the ink-mark, and make your hand come down and come out little by little in turning.
puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit;	then lay your hand in peace, and feel the bone I a small part.
et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit;	and if you do not see it, then begin again the cautery as far as you see the bone as I told you;
aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors;	after take a piece of silk, and put it wet and soft cotton inside, and put on the mark, and leave it three days;
aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre;	then put over the cotton dry wax;
et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	and leave it as long as it is hot enough to be bone;
aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	then heal the wound of the ointment which is called 'tetrarchafarmacon', until it is healthy.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge;	And say the old man that as long as the wound stays open, it will smell more.
et por ce si aide mues.	and so that help is given.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	And they said that one should let the fire cautery burn so long that a part of the bone is burned, and then resect what is burned from the bone, and be healed.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors;	and so that the other can be cauterized as much as possible on top of it, and pressed so strongly that the humor is forced out as much as a woman puts in her vagina to prevent the flow of fluids.
et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte;	and we must leave the wound open for a long time;
aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	afterwards, one must heal and support.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor;	And these two ways of cauterizing do not seem good to me in any way or another, except that in some people there is a possibility of fear;
et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier;	and it seems to me that I should leave it as it is;
car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres;	because the head is weakened by continuous solutions of this nature, as we have witnessed in other members;
et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	and even when the head of the sick is weak by nature, and the first look at the cauterization is safer and more gentle for me, and from that I carry out the whole treatment in a way that saves and heals;
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	of the child's pain at the head
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres;	When in all the head comes chronic pain, and lasts a long time, then the patient must use herbs and pills which are called "cochier", and head purgatives and oils and poultices;
et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	and if they make the fire cautery that we have said above, and it does not work.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit;	Take care that the patient's head is of strong nature, and that he is not too cold;
adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	then cauterize it with fire a little less than what we have said above.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»;	Afterwards make the fire cautery on each horn of the head up to the bone, as we have said above, and make the fire cautery where it is called "vesselz";
et est I leus en coi on met ventouses;	and put them in places where vacuum cups are placed;
et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os:	and adjust your hand so that you do not see the bone at all:
li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors;	The patient feels an intense amount of pain in this fire cautery compared to others, and I will not speak further about it.
et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	And it is necessary that the cornet cauterizations be thinner than those with which we cauterize the top of the head, and this is the form:
dou cautere dou chief	Dou cautere dou chief
Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie:	When sudden pain in one part of the head appears and extends to the oil, and the shoulder is cleaned with medicinal alcohol, and the other treatments I mentioned in the section on diseases are performed, then none of it helps.
adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	Therefore, perform the cauterization in two ways: with medicinal alcohol and fire.
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir;	The cauterization with medicinal alcohol is performed by pressing a piece of wood onto the shoulder, and then removing it twice, and then applying the alcohol to the skin in such a way that you can remove the wood without pain.
et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres;	and when it has been reset, if the bandage and restraint are good and left like this for 12 hours;
et puis le deslie et trait fuers la doce d’ail, et laisse la plaie ensi II jors ou III;	and then unbandage and treat with garlic extract, and leave the wound like this for 2 or 3 days;
puis met sus cotun plongiet en burre tant que porreture en isse.	and then put cotton dipped in butter on it as long as it can become dry again.
Aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	After the treatment with ointment until it is healed;
et se tu vues si fai ceu d’aucunes medicines comburans que j’ai escrites ou dozime traitier des medicines comburans.	and if you see which of the curative medicines I have written or any other treatment for burning.
Li cautere de fer si est selonc ceste meniere.	The fire cautery if it is according to this manner.
Chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Heat the cauterizer with this shape:
Et est apelez «clos» por ceu que li chief est fait a la forme d’un clo ou il ait I poc de corbeure, et em mileu a une petite apparance;	And is called "close" for the head is made in the form of a cloak or it has a small hole of cuirasse, and in the middle to a small appearance;
et le met sor le leu dolorous, et tien ta main et trestorne le feir un poc legierement, tant que li moitiez de l’espés dou keur soit arse;	and sets it on the painful place, and holds your hand and turns the fire slightly, so that half of the heat from the cure is burned;
et lieve ta main que li artere n’arde, que est defuers, et decorre habundance de sanc.	and hold my hand so that the artery does not burn, which is far away, and runs a lot of blood.
Aprés met coton en awe de seil, et met sor le leu par III jors;	After putting cotton in place with thread, and keeping it in place for three days;
puis i met coton moilliet em burre, et puis cure le leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	then I put cotton that is wet in the wound, and then I treat the injury with ointment until it heals;
et se tu vuelz cauterize ceste emigraine avec le cautere qui est apelez «cultellare», a tout la pointe, et te garde de coper l’artere en ceste emigraine qui n’est mie anciaine.	and if you want to cauterize this headache with the cautery that is called "cultellare", do it at the tip, and be careful not to cover the artery in this headache that is not old.
de emigraine	of migraine
Quant tu cures emigraine si com nos avons devant dit en divisions des maladies, et ne profite mie, et vois que li cauteres devant dis de la medicine et dou fer ne li soffit mie, adonques covient il que tu eschaufes le cautere qui est apelez «cultellare» tant qu’il soit blans;	When you treat a headache as we have said before in the division of diseases, and do not benefit from it, and see that the cautery that is called "cultellare" in front of the medicine and does not sufocate it, then it is necessary to heat the cautery that is called "cultellare" until it is white;
et seigne ainsois sor le leu doillant une ligne de demi doi de lonc, et oste ta main une fois, et l’estrain que tu ne coper l’artere et que ne viegnes jusc’a l’os;	and so thus on the shoulder a line of half a foot long, and with your hand once, and pull it so that you do not cover the artery and come no closer than the bone;
et te warde de la mandibule que muet quant on menjut, et li ners n’ait regart que la muet et que spasmus ne veigne a malaide, et te warde de decorrement de sanc de l’artere quant elle sera copee, ou copement ait grant paour et meismement a celui que ne s’i conoit, et qui n’est estudians et esprovez;	and so also on the jaw that moves when chewing, and let it rest only so that the muscle moves and not the spasm comes to the disease, and guard against the blood flowing from the artery when it is cut, or if it has a great fear and least understood, and who is not learned and proven;
et laisse l’uevre em mi voie;	and leave the work half done;
mais je vos dirai coment on restainche sanc quant li artere est copee, et je vos mostrerai a leu ou il afiert en cest livre.	but I will tell you how to stop blood when the artery is cut, and I will show you at what place it occurs in this book.
Et se tu vois que cist cauteres ne soffise mie a la maladie, et li malaides est soffrans, cauterize le enmi le chief ausi com nos avons dit, et cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And if you see that these fire cauterizations do not suffice to the disease, and the patient is suffering, cauterize it in the head as well as we have said, and cure the wound until it heals;
et se tu vues, aministre le cautere que nos avons dit ou chapistre de l’estraction de l’artere, avec le cautere qui ait II coutelz;	and if you see, administer the cautery that we have said or the chapitre for the extraction of the artery, with the cautery that has II knives;
et est cist cauteres millors de celui et plus aidans.	and this cautery is better than that and more helpful.
de la dolor des oreilles de part froidor	for the pain of ears from cold
Quant en l’oreille vient dolor de froit, et on i a ovreit de medicines solutives et des autres cures que nos avons dit en la division, et li dolors ne se muet, adonques eschaufe cest cautere qui est apelez «poins», de coi ci est li forme:	When pain in the ears comes from cold, and medicine or other treatments we mentioned in the division do not help, then this cautery which is called "poins" should be used, whose form is:
Aprés pointoie tout entor l’oreille malaide, ou entor les II se la dolor tient en ambedous, et t’esloigne un poc ensus de la racine de l’oreille puis que tu as signiet le leu d’enche;	After poking all around the sick ear, or around the two of them where the pain is in both, and you distance a little from the root of the ear then because you have found the place of pain;
et ait X poins entor chescune oreille;	and it has ten points poking around each ear;
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After healing the place as long as it is healthy.
de la torture de la bouche	of the mouth torture
Torture qui doit estre curee par cautere nen est fuers que de celles que muevent de fleume, si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladie;	The torture that must be healed by cautery is not stronger than those that move with a flux, as we have said in the division of diseases;
et ne faire point de cautere as semblances que vienent de sechor et de spame de ners.	and do not make any cauterization of doubt that comes from thorns and poison of netherworld.
Quant tu cures ceste semblance de torture qui muet de fleume d’ydres et d’espurgemens de chief et de gargarisme, et ceu ne vaut, adonc covient que tu cauterizes le malaide de III cauteres:	When you treat this pain of the throat, which is moved by the fluid of the yore and by the purgations of the head and gargling, and that does not cease, then it is necessary that you cauterize the patient with three cauterizations:
l’une en la racine de l’oreille, et l’autre un poc defuers la temple, et le tier en l’ajostement des II levres;	one at the root of the ear, and another a little further back from the temple, and the third at the junction of the two lips;
et met le cautere en la partie qui apert saine, et li fai cautere endroit le chief de l’oreille desus un poc desoz la corne dou chief, et un autre en la temple ausi longe com uns poce;	and place the cautery in the healthy part, and make a cauterization on the top of the ear just above the horn of the ear, and another one a little way back from the temple;
et laisse le cautere tant sus que li moitiez dou keur soit arse;	and leave the cautery in place until half of the burn is burned;
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	this is the form of the cauterization:
Et est li semblance dou cutellaire que nos avons mise devant, mais il est un poc plus subtilz et covient que li coutelz soit un poc plus gros;	And this is the form of the scalpel that we have described before, but it is a little finer and it is necessary that the blade be a little thicker;
aprés cure lou leu si com j’ai devant dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After care, let him be as I have said before, until he is well.
Quant apoplexie est ancieinne et tu la cures ensi com nos avons dit, et il ne profite mie, et li malaides n’ait fievre, adonques li fai IIII cauteres:	When apoplexies are old and you treat them in this way as we have said, and they do not benefit, and the patient has no fever, then make four fire cauterizations:
II sus les II cornes dou chief, et I emmi le chief, et I ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz» si com nos avons devant dit, et lou derrien cautere sus la bouche de l’estomac;	II. On the two horns of the head, and I cut off the hair, and I make a hole in it which is called "vessel", as we have said before, and then cauterize the mouth of the stomach;
et soit curez si com nos avons dit devant.	and let him be cured as we have said before.
de litargie	of limestone
A cest maladie covient doner au malaide yeres grans et pilules mondifians le cerveil;	This is a disease that gives the patient great years and pills that hurt the brain;
aprés reis lou chief dou malaide tout, et li met sus l’occipite l’emplaustre de sinapi qui est escrit ou traitier des emplastres;	After cutting off the head of the patient completely, and placing on his occiput the dye of mustard which is written or treated with dyes for plasters;
et c’est li maniere dou cautere:	and this is the way of the cauterization:
si lou fai si com j’ai dit.	If I do so as I have said.
S’il est sanez ensi, boin est;	If he is well thus, it is good.
et s’il ne l’est, se li fai III cauteres des emmi le chief en dessendant jusc’a col, et ait d’espaice entre chescun cautere I doi de gros;	and if he is not well, give him three fire cauterions to the top of his head while descending as far as the collarbone, and leave two inches of space between each cauterization;
et le cure si com les autres, et se tu i vues ajoster, et li malaides est soffrans, se li fai I cautere en mileu;	and the surgeon does so as with the others, and if he sees it move, and the patient suffers, give him one cauterization in the middle;
et se mestiers est, II autres sus les II cornes, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and if that is not enough, two others on top of the two horns, and the surgeon as long as he is well;
et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «olivare», si com j’ai devant dit.	and let the cauterization be called 'oliver', as I have said before.
de la froidor dou chief	of the head
Il covient que li chief soit mundifiez de yeres et de ceu que nos avons devant dit;	It is necessary that the head be cleaned of years and of what we have said above;
aprés reis le chief dou malaide, puis li fai cautere emmi le chief et sus chescune corne, et I derrier et III sus l’espinee dou col;	after he has washed the head of the sick person, then give him a cauterization to the top of his head and to each of the two horns, and one behind and three in the spine of the neck;
et se tu en as plus mestier, et li cors est moiste et li malaides est soffrans, et li maladie est fors, se li fai IIII cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos;	and if you have more need of it, and the heart is moist and the patient suffers, and the disease is severe, then do four fire cauterizations on the spine of the back;
et li laisse tant que li plus dou keur soit ars, et lieve ta main;	and let it be as long as the top of the curl is burned, and raise your hand;
aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez, et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «olivare» que nos avons devant dit.	after the cure as long as he is healthy, and let be the cauterization which is called 'olive' that we have said above.
de l’epilempsie	of epilepsy
Li epilentiques ne doit useir de cautere fuers que cil qui est fleumatique, et covient premier mondifier le cerveil de yeres et d’autres cures que nos avons dites en la division quant li malaides est grans et soffrans de penre medicine.	For the fire cautery, one should only use it on those who are feverish, and first moisten the scalp and perform other treatments we have mentioned in the chapter on treatment when the patient is severe and suffering from heat-based medicines.
Et se c’est uns enfes qui ne lou puisse soffrir, se li fai gargarisme et mastication mondifiant le cerveil sovent avec bones viandes;	And if it is a child who cannot endure the pain, then do gargling and chewing with bone meat often;
aprés li reis lou chief em mileu, et i fai I cautere selonc ce que nos avons dit devant, et I cautere sus lou vassel, et sus chescune corne;	after he has eaten a meal in the middle, and I do one cauterization according to what we have said above, and I do cauterize on the neck, and on each horn;
et se li malaides est fors et soffrans, se li fai cauteres si com j’ai dit a celui qui ait paralisie et mollification de cors, sus l’espinee dou dos et dou col, et soit li cauteres olivier selonc la maniere que j’ai dit.	and if the patient is severe and suffering, then do cauterize as I have said to one who has paralysis and softening of the spine and neck, and let the olive cauterization be done according to the way I have said.
Se li malaides est enfes, se li fai I cautere subtil selonc ceste maniere:	If the patient is blind, then perform the fire cautery according to this manner:
Quant par la cause de melancolie sunt les superfluitez ou les moistors corrumpues et fleume grosse, adonques lou cauterize de teils cauteres com nos avons dit a celui qui ait paralisie.	When due to melancholy there are excesses or corrupt moisture and thick fluid, then lou cauterize partly with the fire cautery as we have said to one who has paralysis.
Et se par la cause de melancolie est li superfluitez declinans a melancolie, et est li cors dou malaide moistes, adonc li done a boivre chose par coi li cervelz soit mundifiez, selonc ceu qu’il est devant en la division.	And if due to melancholy the excesses decline into melancholy, and the patient's body is moist, then he drinks something to cleanse the brain, according to what has been said in the division about it.
Aprés reis lou chief dou malaide;	After the head of the sick person.
aprés fai I torteil de lin bien fait, ausi com I cercle, si le met emmi le chief;	Then I make a turban of fine linen, also as a circle, and put it on the head;
et li malaides sié croisiez, et soit bien tenus de toutes pars;	and I place the sick person so that they are comfortable, and well held together from all sides;
aprés presente le linement, et vaut mues de burre de berbis ancien;	Then present the linen bandage, and be sure to use old butter of sheep's milk;
et lou chaufe a feu tempreement, si que li dois s’on li boute le puisse soffrir;	and the fire is hot, so that it may not harm him if he drinks it;
aprés vuide le cercle par dedens emmi le chief, et lou laisse refroidier;	Then empty the circle inside the turban, and leave it to cool;
et fai ce a malaide chescune semaine une fois avec autre governement boin, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and do this to the sick person every week with good care, until they are well.
Ou se tu vues cauterize lou en faisant poins plusors a tot le cautere.	And if you see fire cautery, make many punctures all over the cauterization.
Ceste maniere de cautere amoistit le cerveil igaument;	This method of cauterization hardens the skull slightly;
et puis met sus coton moilliet en burre et en graisse de geline.	and then put on wet cotton in butter and sheep's milk fat.
de l’awe des eulz	of the eyes
Quant awe vient premierement as eulz par les signes que j’ai dit en la division, adonques encomence et done boivre au malaide chose mundifiant le chief, et le warde de toutes moistors, et lou fai suer ou bain plusors fois a jeun.	When it comes first the eyes by the signs that I have said in the division, then begin and do drink to the patient a thing purifying the skull, and warding away all moisture, and let it sweat or bathe many times while fasting.
Aprés li comande a rere son chief, et li fai cautere emmi le chief, et li fai II cauteres sus les II temples se li dessendemens de l’awe est as II eulz ensamble, ou en I se li dessendemens est en I;	Then instruct him to raise his head, and make a cauterization on the head, and do two cauterizations on the temples if he is able to stand it without pain, or one cauterization if he cannot stand it but can still move his head;
et cope a tout le cautere toutes les voines et les arteres que sont desoz le keur, et soient li cautere lonc selon lou large de la temple;	and bandage all the cautery all the veins and arteries that are outside of the curb, and let the cautery be long according to the width of the temple;
et te warde de decorrement de sanc, et se tu vois trop de sanc issir, si li estainche de teil pooir com tu as.	and guard against the corruption of blood, and if you see too much blood coming out, stop it with a cloth so that it can be stopped with what power you have.
Et je t’enseignerai en l’estraction des arteres et a l’incision la cautele coment tu l’estencheras;	And I will teach you how to cauterize the arteries in extraction and incising, how to stop it;
et aucune fois fait on cautere ou hatereil desoz les II os derrier.	and never do you make a cautery or hate it outside of the two bones behind.
dou cors des larmes	The two courses of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont ancienes et acostumees et sont sus les voines, ou delez les arteres que sont en l’aparance dou chief defors;	When the tears of the eyes are old and accustomed and are on the veins, or choose the arteries that are in appearance on the outside of the head;
et on voit que c’est des superfluitez froides fleumatiques, adonques li fai le cautere que j’ai dit en l’encomencement de l’awe dessendant as eulz:	and it is seen that it is a cold and flaccid superfluity, then make the cautery I mentioned at the beginning of the descent from the eyes:
I cautere emmi le chief, et II cauteres sus les II temples, et II cauteres ou haiterel desoz les II os;	I cauterize my head, and I cauterize on the two temples, and I cauterize where the hair grows on the two bones;
et s’il i a besoigne plus, si le cauterize saigement desus le sorcil a tout I petit cautere.	and if there is more need, if the cautery bleeds slightly above the brow, then cauterize it again with a small cautery.
dou cors des larmes par dedens les eulz	The two courses of tears move inward through the eyes.
Quant tu le medicines selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et il ne profite mie, adonques done a boivre a malaide III nuis cochies;	When you treat it according to what we said in the division, and it does not benefit, then only drink three times of bad wine.
aprés li reis le chief, et li fai cautere ou mileu dou cautere olivaire;	After he has raised his head, and makes a cautery in the middle of the olive oil cautery;
et fai II cauteres dou cautere qui est apelez «clavilis» sus les II sorcis, un poc desoz les chevous;	and make two cauteries on the cautery called "clavilis" on the two brows, a little shaved;
et te warde de l’artere que tu ne la coper.	and be careful of the artery so that you do not cover it.
Et c’est li forme dou cautere qui est apelez «clavilis»:	And this is the form of the cautery that is called “clavis”:
Quant li papiere de l’oil est mollifie de maladie et de moistor, adonques la cautarize de cest cautere qui est apelez «olivare».	When the paper of the oil is softened by disease and moisture, then the cautery of this cautery that is called "olive".
de coi ci est li forme:	for this is the form:
Et se tu vues si fai II cauteres sus les II sorcis ausi lons com li sorcilz sont;	And if you see, make two cauteries on the two brows as long as the eyebrows are;
et n’i lassiez mie la main fors que tant que li tierce partie de la papiere soit arse, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit.	and do not leave my hand free until such time as the third part of the paper is burned, according to the way that I have said.
dou poil qui point l’oil	dou poil qui point l’oil
Aucune fois avient que li poil des oilz sont convertit au pardedens, et poignent l’oil, et i fait on cauteres selonc II manieres:	No sooner had the hair of the loins been converted to the parched state, and having pricked them, we made the cauterization according to two ways:
c’est a savoir de feu, ou de medicine ardant.	either with fire, or with fiery medicine.
Ou cautere de feu comande au malaide qu’il laisse les poilz tant qu’il soient lons et igals;	For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even;
et s’il le poignent a lor nassance, se li estraint les eulz qu’il ne se muevent tant qu’il naissent.	and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Quant il naissent et i sont igalz, adonques met le malaide en ton sain;	When they have grown and are equal, then place the patient in your care;
aprés seigne sus la papiere des eulz une figure que soit ausi com li fuelle dou mirte, et soit li comencemens dou signe delez les poilz;	after signing on the paper of the hairs a figure which is also like the furrow of the palm, and is the beginning of the sign to prick the hairs;
puis i met coton moilliet en glaire d’uef et muscillaige de persillion sus l’oil, puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	then dip cotton in egg white and musk root emulsion over the oil, then heat the cautery so that it is this shape:
Aprés cauterize sus la figure que tu as signiet poc et poc mout de fois, que li keurs soit ars lai endroit;	After cauterizing on the shape you have marked little by little several times, so that the wound heals in place;
et li signes de la santeit de l’uevre est que tu voies la papiere retraite, et les poilz levez a la pointure de l’oil;	and the sign of the health of the work is that you see the paper withdraw, and the hairs stand up to the point of the oil;
adonques lieve ta main, et laisse ensi III jors, puis i met coton moilliet en burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	then take your hand away, and leave it like this for three days, then dip cotton in butter as the cauterization heats up;
aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the cauterization treatment until it is healthy.
Et se aprés ceu vienent li poilz, et li papiere est mollifie adonques rencomence le cautere sus cel leu meisme, si com tu as fait premiers;	And if after this come the hairs, and the paper is softened then start cauterizing on top again, just like you did first;
et se li poil sont defuer, si le cauterize tant que li papiere soit levee a son leu natureil, et soit igals, et ne poignent mie li poil l’oil.	and if the hairs have gone, then cauterize so that the paper returns to its natural position, and is even, and do not touch the hairs to the oil.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il laisse les poilz tant qu’il soient grans et igalz, puis fai de parchemin la forme de la foille de mirte;	The fire medicine cauterizes wounds by ordering the patient to let their hair grow long and even. Then, make a parchment in the shape of a laurel leaf.
puis pren de savon fransois et de vive chalz, de chescun une .З., et broie ensamble bien;	Then, take French soap and hot water, each a .Z., and mix them well together;
et le fai hastanment, si qu’il ne refroide, puis en espant sus la forme que tu es fait sicom la foille dou mirte, et met sus la papiere des eulz;	and apply it immediately, so that it does not cool down, then spread it over the parchment of the hairs;
et se li maladie tient en I oil soulement, si doit on ovrer en I, et se en ambedous ausi;	and if the disease only affects one side, then you must operate on that side, and in the same way on the other side as well;
et met desoz l’oil coton moilliet en abin d’uef;	and cover it with a moist cotton cloth;
et li chiés dou malaide soit en ton sain et met ton doi mostrant sus la medicine, et presse I poc et lou muef toutes les fois que li malaide sent mordication de la medicine, car il sent mordication ausi com de feu.	and the dislocated shoulder should be in your sound side; place the medicine on it, and press it slowly and gently each time the patient feels a burning sensation from the medicine, as he also feels a burning sensation like fire.
Quant tu as ceu fait longement, si oste la medicine a ton doit.	If you have had this for a long time, take the medicine to your mouth.
Et quant li mordication sera passee, si leve le leu d’awe, et rewarde se tu vois la papiere levee ausi com s’ele estoit levee par constraignement de feu ou par incision;	And when the swelling has passed, then raise the head of bed, and keep an eye on whether the paper is raised as if it were raised by the constriction of fire or by an incision.
et s’il est ensi, si est bien.	and if so, well done.
Se ceu non, si remet encor de la medicine sus lou leu ou li medicine n’ait ovreit, tant que tes ovraiges soit igalz, et tes eulz mis a point;	if not, then continue with the medicine on the bed or wherever it has reached, until your hair is even and combed.
puis met sus coton moilliet en burre tant que li keurs ars soit cheus, aprés cure le leu de l’oignement qui est apelez «dyafenis» et d’autre, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then put cotton wetted with balm on it as long as the wound hurts, after treating the head of the injury called "dyafenis" and others, until it is well.
Et se t’est mestier que tu te warde bien a ton ovraige par grant warde qu’il ne chiece point de la medicine as eulz.	And if you have to take care of your wound with great care so that the medicine does not touch the hairs.
Et se li papiere devient mole aprés, et li poil poignent en l’oil, si recomence la medicine sus celui leu qui est mollifiez de la papiere proprement, ensi com tu as fait devant;	And if the paper becomes soft then, and the hair pricks into the oil, then begin again with the medicine on that very same head that has been softened by the paper, in the same way that you did before;
aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	after treating until it is well.
et c’est li forme de la fuelle dou mirte:	and this is the form of the furrow in the breast:
Et saichés que li eul des homes sont divers en grandor et en petitece, et selonc ceu soit tes constraignemens;	You must know that men's breasts are various in size and shape, and according to this.
et ne soit mie reponue li droite voie a celui cui est li estude de cest art.	and it should not be repeated the right way to those whose business is this craft.
de la cure de fistule par cautere	Of the cure of a fistula by cautery
Quant tu cures fistule si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladies, et tes cures ne profitent mie, adonques covient il que tu li fais cautere selonc ceste maniere.	When you treat a fistula as we have said in the division of diseases, and your treatment does not benefit them, then it is necessary that you apply cauterization according to this method.
Comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain;	Command the sick person to put his head in your lap;
et teigne li menistres son chief entre tes mains en teil maniere qu’il ne se mueve, ne ne demoinne son chief;	and place the patient's hair between your thumbs so that it does not move or tumble;
aprés met coton moilliet en abin d’uef ou en jus de persillion sus l’oil;	afterwards, dip cotton in oil of aloes or in juice of pomegranate on the oil;
aprés chaufe le cautere qui est teilz:	afterwards, heat the fire-iron which is sharp;
et est chevez au chief si com li forme d’une penne de vouteul, ensamble la queil soit li cautere;	and place the iron on the head as if it were the shape of a dove's beak, together let the fire-iron be;
se tu vues, si soit apointé des l’un chief dusc’a l’autre, et se tu vues, si soit ausi com une tente;	if you see, if it is pointed at one end from the other, and if you see, if it is also as a tent;
mais toutevoie, cist qui est chevez vaut mues por ton ovraige.	but moreover, he who is head of his work must move because of your work.
Aprés presse la fistule s’ele est overte, et en trai la porriture, et la seche;	After pressing the fistula has opened, and in it train the porridge, and dry;
et s’ele est close, si la oevre, et trai fuers la bowe;	and if it is closed, if you work, and train hard the bowels;
aprés met sus le cautere chaut forment, et tien ta main au cautere a la partie dou neif ensus de l’oil, que ta mains ne faice folie;	After put on the fire the hot-water pot, and hold your hand to the pot at the part below the oil, that your hand does not make foolishness;
et met le cautere en la graisse de l’oil, et la corromp.	and put the fire in the oil fat, and corrupt it.
Se tu viens au comencement dou cautere jusc’a l’os, si serait bien.	If you come to the beginning of cauterization just to the bone, it would be good.
Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors;	If not, if you restart the fire again, and another you have need, and let it be for three days;
aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers;	After I put on cotton wet in butter, and the cure of the infection dry as long as it is healthy, and forty days pass that it is not healthy, then put on medicine bitter as long as the bone is uncovered;
et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	and let him come according to what he will come in his chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	And I have a way of cauterizing fistulas, which no one of the ancients said.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu;	Listen to the fistula, and cut off the place.
aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	After that, put fine steel in it so that this is the shape:
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc;	and I make the quantity of one .Z. of plaster;
et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil;	and hold it firmly with your hand, and do not move the patient so that the melted plaster does not run to its oil;
et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe:	and it is necessary that one put on the patient cotton moistened in wine or ale;
li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	the plaster so that he covers the place of the fistula, and the sound by a wonderful health.
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	And if the fistula is healed by the cauterization which we have said, it is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	But if not, then a piece of iron should be administered to the nose, and the fistula brought back to the nose's own place according to what should be done in its own place.
des crevaices en levres	crevasses in lips
Mout de fois avienent crevaices en levres que sont apelees «poil», et meismement en levres des enfans.	times have creases in the lips, which are called "hair", and most often in the lips of adults.
Quant tu cures ces crevaices de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et li cure ne profite, adonques eschaufe I petit cautere cultellaire selonc ceste forme:	When you treat these creases as we have said in the divisions, and the cure does not benefit, then heat a small caustice according to this form:
Et le met hastanment en celles crevaices tant qu’il viegne jusc’a font;	And put it carefully in those crevices until it comes to the end of the hole;
aprés cure le leu de cerote tant qu’il soit sanez.	After that, treat the place of the wound with ointment as long as it is well.
de l’aposteme de la goule	of the abscess of the throat
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule;	When an abscess develops at the root of the gullet or the uvula or the palate or at the roots of the teeth, after fermentation and rotting and has become swollen and becomes a fistula;
et tu le cures si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie:	and you cure it as we have said in the division, and it is no benefit:
adonques covient il que tu aies I cautere selonc la quantiteit de la fistule;	then you must have the cautery according to the quantity of the fistula;
aprés le bote ou pertus de la fistule, et tien ta main tant que li fer chaus viegne au font de li, et ou derrien leu;	after the bottle or hole of the fistula, and hold your hand until the fire comes to the edge of it, and where it goes down;
et fai ensi une fois ou II, aprés le cure de ce que nos avons dit en cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and make this once or twice after the cure we have said, until he is well;
et s’il est curez ensi, c’est boin;	and if it is cured in this way, it is good;
et se ceu non, si covient descovrir le leu et oster l’os corrumput, selonc ceu que vos le troverez en son chapistre.	and if not, if it is necessary to uncover the place and remove the corrupted bone, according to what you will find in his chapter.
dou movement des dens	the movement of teeth
Quant les gencives sont mollifies par moistor et les dens muevent, et tu le cures per medicines et ceu ne vaut, adonc met le chief dou malaide en ton sain;	When the gums are softened by moisture and the teeth move, and you cure it with medicine and that does not work, then put the head of the sick in your healthy one;
aprés eschaufe le cautere dont li forme venra ci aprés en teil maniere que tu mettes une cainne sor le dent;	After heating the fire cautery, its shape will come out in a certain way that you put a chain on the teeth;
et met dedens le cautere chaut hastanment, et tien tant ta main que li malaides sente la chalor venant a la racine dou dent;	and place the heated fire cautery inside, and hold it for so long that the sick person feels the heat coming from the root of the teeth;
aprés lieve ta main et rencomence le cautere selonc ta volenteit;	After removing your hand and starting again with the cauterization according to your will;
aprés emplisse li malaides sa bouche d’awe salee, et la teigne une houre et raiche fuers.	After filling the mouth of the sick person with foul salt, and rinsing it thoroughly for an hour.
Et en teil maniere li dens qui estoit movans si est confermez, et li gencive mollifie restrainte, et li moistors corrumpue sechie.	In such a way that the tooth that was moving is confirmed, and the gums that were softened are dried up, and the moisture that corrupts is dried out.
de la dolor des dens	of tooth pain
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres:	When the toothache comes from cold, or there is coldness or swelling, and medicines do not work, then it is necessary to use fire cauterization in two ways:
et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	and fire cautery.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain;	and fire cautery if it is such that you squeeze butter from a cow, and the end in a spoon of iron or bronze;
aprés pren coton et envolope sus la pointe d’une tente, et la moille en burre bulit, et met sus le dent dolant hastanment et tien tant qu’il soit refroidiez;	after take cotton and wrap it on the tip of a tent, and the juice in butter that is made, and put on the tooth with great care and hold it until it has cooled down;
et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	and then often as long as its virtue comes to the root of the tooth, and if you see that wet wool and cotton make butter cool, and put it on the aching tooth, and put it on a hot iron as long as the fire comes to the tooth channel.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide;	The fire cautery together if it is such that you squeeze a iron or bronze wire, and be thick so that the fire does not come to the mouth of the sick person;
aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez;	After you have heated the cautery, so that it forms as described here, place it on the tooth and hold your hand until the cautery has cooled.
fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	do this often, for the pain will increase by midday or the next day.
Et covient que li malaides emplisse sa bouche de boin burre en l’empressement de cel cautere, et puis le raiche fuer;	And it is necessary that the patient fill his mouth with good butter in the hurry for that cautery, and then swallows it.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	this is how you do the cautery:
Et fai cautere dou queil chief que tu voudras, et selonc ceu que tu as pooir;	and make the cautery on the middle of the tooth that you wish, and according to what you have power;
et c’est li forme de la caine:	this is how you do the cautery on the edge of the tooth:
des scrophules	of scrofula
Quant les scrophules sont de fleume et de moistors froides, et ne sont obeissans a digestion par medicines, adonques eschaufe le cautere cheveit de coi ci aprés vient li forme, et ait II aovertures por les fumees a issir au cautere de l’autre partie;	When the abscesses are of cold moisture and do not submit to digestion by medicines, then heat the cautery as described above, and make two openings for the fumes to come out on one side of the tooth with this cautery, and on the other side with that.
et met le cautere chaut sus l’apostume une fois, ou II se mestier est, tant qu’il viegne au font de l’apostume;	and apply the fire cautery repeatedly over the abscess as long as it reaches the bottom of the abscess;
et se li apostume est petis si met cautere selonc la quantiteit de l’apostume, et le laisse ensi III jors;	and if the abscess is small, apply cautery in proportion to the quantity of the abscess and leave it like this for three days;
et met sus coton moilliet em burre tant que li arsure soit ostee;	and put cotton wet with oil on it until the burn is completely healed;
aprés cure le leu d’oignemens et de tentes tant qu’il soit sanez.	after treatment, apply the ointment and bandage until it is well;
Li forme de la cainne:	The form of the cane:
Quant les moistors vainquent sus les chenals dou pormon, et meismement quant ce vient de froide complexion, adonc covient que li malaides soit voidiez premiers par medicines solutives;	When the moisture overtakes the shoulder blade, and most importantly when it comes from a cold complexion, then the patient must be emptied first with giải thuốc giải độc;
aprés li fai cautere a la racine de la gorge, et te garde que tu ne venir mie jusc’a la gorge, et n’ardre dou keur mais c’un poc.	after the fire cautery at the root of the throat, and be careful not to go any further than the throat, and don't burn it more than a grain;
Aprés li fai I autre cautere a la jointure dou col au chief de l’espinee, et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» de coi nos avons la forme devant;	After the fire cautery at the joint of the neck at the base of the spine, and let the cautery that is called 'clavicle' be there, so we have the shape in front;
et cure le leu si com nos avons devant dit tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat the lunge as we have said before until it is healthy.
de la toust	of the toast
Quant tous et maladie de pormon sont de moistors froides, et li malaides nen ait fievre ne sechor, et est li maladie anciaine, se li fai .II cauteres sus la forcele en leus vuis;	When all and the disease of the foot are cold moisture, and the patient does not have a fever or itchiness, and the disease is old, then do cauterization on the sole of the foot;
et I autre cautere emmi le pis entre II mameles;	and another cautery burn between the breasts;
et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» selonc la forme qui est devant dite.	and let the cauterization be called "clavicle" according to the form which has been said before.
Et se tu vues, fai cautere en poignant a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins» de coi li forme est ci devant en la maladie des oreilles;	And if you see, make a cauterization by poking at all the cauterization which is called "poins" so that the form is as before in the disease of the ears;
et soient li poins jusc’a XXX, ou enqui entor.	and let the pokes be only up to thirty, or less.
Aprés cure le leu selonc ceu qui est devant dit, et soit li cauteres a III rains selonc ceste forme:	Afterward, treat the hole according to what is mentioned above, and let the cauterization be made with three rains according to this form:
Et por ceu sont li cautere plus legier, por ceu que tu en fais III a cop.	And for those where the cauterization is lighter, for which you make three together.
de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the dislocation of the shoulder
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.
Aprés soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos et sus son costeit;	Afterwards, instruct the patient to stretch on their back and side;
aprés lieve le keur qui est dedens le titillite as dois de ta main senestre;	Afterward, give a slap with two fingers of your left hand;
et se li jointure est desaluee dedens, si eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners douqueil ci est li forme:	and if his joint is dislocated from within, then heat the fire at the top of the body as follows:
et cauterize lou keur tant qu’il le perce jusc’a costeit, et venrait li fugure dou cautere ensamble IIII cauteres;	and cauterize it until he pierces to the ribs and joins together four cauterizes.
et por ceu est faite cautere avec le cautere qui a III ners, por coi li figure de cauterization sunt sis cauteres;	and for this, cauterize with the fire that has three sides, so that the shape of cauterization is six cauterizes.
et sont li nerf selonc la subtiliteit d’une tente et c’est li forme dou cautere qui a III ners:	and let the nerve follow the subtlety of a thread and this is the form of the fire that has three sides:
Et aucune fois est ajostez sus ce I nerf por coi il i a VIII cauteres.	And never place on this nerve because there are eight cauteries.
Aprés met sus le cautere porrelz broiez avec seil;	After, place the fire on the fire for three hours with sea salt;
aprés fai reposer le malaide, et ne soit meus li membres par lonc tens tant qu’il soit bien confortez.	After, let the patient rest and do not move his limbs for a long time until he is well comforted.
Et s’il est desaloiez desus, liquelz chose avient poc, adonques fait cautere sus l’epaisse dou cautere clavile, ou mout de cauteres en poignant.	And if it is dislocated again, let the following thing happen; then make a cauterization with the thick ring of fire, or a large number of cauteries pierce it.
Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	For the joint is closed, and the moisture is dried up, and the patient is healed.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	When in the stomach there come chills and moisture until it is removed from its color, and are multiplied to him the catharres, and are manners of accustomed cures and he does not benefit, then the patient should be made to lie on his back, and extend his legs and hands.
De ceu en aprés li fai III cauteres I desoz la cuillier dou pis per la quantiteit d’un doi, a tout le cautere clavile, et II cauteres defuers les II costez tant que li figure des cauteres soit a III angles, et ait teil espaice entre l’une et l’autre qu’elles ne soient jointes ensamble quant elles giteront porriture;	From this, then, make three cauterizes with the knife of the foot, all four cauterize, and two cauterizes on the sides as far as the form of the cauterizes is at three angles, and there must be a space between them so that they do not join together when they burn;
et soient li cautere si parfont qu’il porpreignent les II pars dou keur, et soit li figure des cauteres selonc ceste forme sens ajostement:	and let the cauterization be so perfect that it purifies the two parts of the cure, and let the shape of the cauterization be according to this form without adjustment:
Et se tu vues cauterize d’un grant cautere enmi l’estomac selonc ceste forme;	And if you cauterize with a large cautery the stomach according to this form;
et celui qui avra paour de cest cautere, cauterize en poignant et seigne sus l’estomac i. point selonc la quantiteit que tu vues d’enche;	and he who has fear of this cautery, cauterize by poking and signing on the stomach at a point according to the quantity that you see fit;
puis le cauterize a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins».	then cauterize all the cauterization that is called "point".
Aprés le cure de la cure que nos avons eut devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the cure of the wound that we had before, as long as he is healthy.
Quant au foie vient dolor de froit et de moistor et de grosse ventositeit, tant qu’il est fuer mis de sa complexion natureil per les superfluitez;	As for the liver, it comes with pain from cold and moisture and a great windiness, as much as it is forcibly taken out of its natural condition because of excesses;
et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne li profite mie, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son haitereil;	and the patient is cured of what we have said in divisions, and it does not benefit him if he abstains from his dietary restrictions;
et signe d’enche III cauteres selonc ceste forme et ceste figure et ceste quantiteit sus lou foie, defuer les ypocondres, lai ou li coutes de l’ome vient;	and a mark of three cauterizations according to this form and this figure and this quantity on the liver, away from the hypochondriums, where the cut of the womb comes;
et ait d’espaice entre chaicun cautere la groissece d’un doi;	and space between each cauterization the thickness of two fingers;
et soient li cautere dou lonc dou cors, et ne presser mie mout ta main a tot le cautere;	and be the cauterization of the long neck, and do not press my hand all the way down to the whole cauterization;
et soit arse tant soulement li moitiez dou keur, et soit li malaides drois sus ses piez;	and let it burn only halfway down the root, and be the patient right-side-up on his feet;
et s’il ne peut, si soit gisans, et estende ses jambes, et lieve ses brais;	and if he cannot, if he is sitting, and extends his legs, and raises his breasts;
et c’est li forme:	this is the form:
Et se ta volentez est, si cauterize ces cauteres dou cutellaire, se tu es subtilz et saiges en l’art, et te warde que tu n’ardes mie tout le keur, car tu feroies sechier tout le cors;	And if your will is, if you cauterize these cauterizations of the root, if you are subtle and wise in the art, and you guard that you do not burn all the way down, for you would dry out all the body;
et qu’il ne viegne jusc’a boueil, car li keurs est mout subtilz lai endroit, et lou saiches por voir.	and it does not come out until it is hot, for the cur is very subtle in that place, and let's see.
Quant il a apostume au foie, et tu vues savoir s’il est en la char dou foie ou en la toile:	When there is an abscess in the liver, and you can see if it is in the parenchymatous tissue or in the capsule:
s’il est en la char, se sent li malaides dolor ne mie trop fort;	if it is in the parenchyma, the patient feels pain that is not too strong;
et s’il est en la toile, si sent dolor forsenee.	and if it is in the capsule, one feels sudden pain.
Et lors quant ceste cure desoit les mires, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus sa teste;	And then when this treatment has finished, the patient must be careful not to move his head too much;
et puis seigne d’enche le leu ou li apostumes est, et puis chaufe le cautere qui est semblans au rais, de coi ci est li forme:	and then sign with a finger where the abscess is, and then heat the fire cautery that looks like a pin, so as to form:
Et cauterize I cautere tant que li keurs soit ars, et viegne jusc’a syphac, tant que li porreture soit toute fuers;	and cauterize until the cur is burned, and it comes out little by little, until the pus is all gone.
aprés la cure selonc la cure des essues tant qu’il soit sanez;	After the cure according to the cure of the scabs until he is healthy;
et ne covient mie que de cest cautere use nuls fuers que cil qui ait estudieit longement en l’art de medicine, et par cui mains cestes maladies ont corrut aucune fois.	and it only works for those who have studied medicine for a long time and by whom these diseases have not been corrupted once.
Adonques puet il hardiement ovrer, et toutevoies il me semble que mues vaut li laissier.	And then it can take hard work, and always I think that we should leave him.
dou cautere de pleuresin	For the plaudits of pleurisy:
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere:	The old people said that one should use roots of aristolochia as cauterization, and in a certain way:
pren une racine d’aristologe longe, la plus grant que tu poras troveir, et soit seche, et soit ausi grosse et ausi longe comme tes dois;	take a long root of aristolochia, the largest you can find, and dry it, and also make it as thick and as long as your two hands;
et la moille en oile, et l’emprens au feu, et cauterize I cautere entre la forcele et lou col, et II petis cauteres un poc en dessendant en la partie qui est desoz la barbe;	and soak it in oil, and hold it over the fire, and cauterize one small cauterization between the jaw and the neck, and two small cauterizations in going down into the part which is diseased;
et II cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc;	and two cauterizations between the fifth rib and the sixth, in going back a little;
et I cautere emmi le pis, et I autre sus l’estomac, et I entre II espaules, et II as II costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre II espaules;	and cauterize the anus, and another on the stomach, and between the two shoulders, and under the two shoulders there is cautery that comes between the two shoulders;
et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	and do not press my hand, but rather open it widely as in smelling.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme;	And no one old said that any man uses fire cautery resembling the razor, and he blows it up and puts it between the ribs, as far as it comes to the apoplexy;
et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	and so forward with pain, as we have said in the apoplexy of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work there is fear that the patient will die now, or a fistula comes from which cannot be healed.
de la mice	of the mouse
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the disease of the mouse, as we have said in the division of treatments, and it does not benefit, then they have three ways of fire cautery that are all good.
