Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	From which there is a way that you do three cauterizations, or four, in drawing according to the length of the mouse, according to the shape of the fire cautery of the liver that we have said before;
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	and do not press your hand on all the cauterization, and let the patient turn over on his back;
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	and another way to cauterize is that you heat the cautery which has two sides, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder;
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and place the knife which is on the patient's left side, where the cut comes from the left, and be the elevation that you place the knife according to the knife, according to the length of the body, and the cautery is according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	Afterwards pour on the two sides with fire until the knife is perceived from the other side, and then quickly remove the cautery, and so you will have four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you want, cauterize the whole with three sides of the cautery.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the cure has gotten worse over a long time, and this is true that the other before said cure must be used.
de ydropisie	about dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cautery does not suit yropic, except for the way that is called "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you cure it according to the ways that we have said in divisions, and your cure does not benefit, then it is necessary that you do four cauterizations around the loins, and one on the stomach, and one on the liver, and one on the left side, and two behind the back on the spine, and one on the right foot;
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cautery be well placed on the skin's surface.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	After leave the fire cautery open for to go away long time, and don't let the treatment of the sick after the cautery;
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and the healing would hurry up, and both intentions would be together with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The form of the cautery for the belly is the nail that we have in front of us to pull out;
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and this for the back is olive-colored, according to what it is put forward.
de l’enfleure des piez	of swelling of the parts
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in the person who is ydropic, and they are plain of yellow color, you must cauterize on the back of the foot between the index and the middle finger;
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	and move your hand with the fire cautery without turning it back.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not go too deep in the part, otherwise it would come out white; and make the cauterization according to this shape:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After make on the two legs two cauteries in each leg at the point of the knife;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and let the caustics be long, one behind the hip and the other forward, between the legs;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the caustics on for a long time without treating, that they may work;
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	after the treatment of the other treatments that we have said.
de la menoison	of the house
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When the solution of the stomach comes from cold and moisture, as long as the virtues retain and digest that are in the stomach and in the intestines are afflamed, and cannot be cured by any kind of treatment;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you will see the patient very suffering and of great virtue, so make I grant the caustic on the stomach according to what he has spoken before or the caustic of the stomach, at the caustic circle;
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and four caustics within the subtle bud to any caustic in the subtle key, and two caustics on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see moisture abundant and the patient suffering, then make fire cautery on his knuckle, and I cautery on each finger, and II small cauteries in the stomach of the great, for the remedy is profitable when there is good assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	For the cure of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When the hemorrhoids are at the base or one or more, and are old and of large cold and moist corrupted humors, and are cured as we have said in the divisions, and do not profit if cauterization is done:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	To the spine at the back, that which is completely destroyed should be cut little by little in a triangular shape, and cauterize the two bones.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	and if you think that his stomach is cold, and the meat does not cook, and one can see swelling on the face, then the face is cauterized all over with fire, as said before, and another on the liver, and another on the bile all over the body is cauterized;
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and leave the fire cautery open for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	Aftercare until he is healthy again.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	from the charnosity which is called “theloële”
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you cut the abscess, if you heat the fire that seems like a razor, and then put it all ablaze on the cut abscess;
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and I leave your hand so that the cauterization comes to the birth of the vein, from which it is uncut.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this once or twice, and if there is moisture of the armpit, cauterize each one as we have said;
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after the cures of ointments that are profitable until they are healthy;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a large fire on the armpit, it will be more helpful.
de plaie mal curee	from a wound that has not been treated well
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure cutting or opening, which we will tell you in your place, if it comes to a disease that cannot be healed except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there is no outlet for the vent, and it is inflamed and produces pus and corruption, then you should provide a complete thin paste, and be sure to know exactly how much of the paste is required.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After heating the cautery that seems to be sharp, and filling it with fire in the fistula according to the quantity that it seems to have entered, and then restart the cauterization as many times as those infected and corrupt parts of the body burn, once or twice or three times, according to the quantity of the need;
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and be careful of the nerves that are inside, and great veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	If there is a fistula in the torso of the bladder and intestine, be careful with these veins, and do not make incisions except in the middle part, and think that it is not forever.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	After treating the wound as long as it is healthy, and if the veins are sewed up, and the matter is ossified for a long time, then know that the wound is completely healed;
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the matter is not ossified, know that the wound is divided in two, and the bone is corrupted at the root;
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and thus as one of these things that we will say in its place.
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When the pain of frost comes with rain and strong wind, and does not respond to women's remedies, then you must apply a fire cautery on both sides of the rain with the key-shaped cautery that we have mentioned above;
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if we cauterize it with milk, there will be three cauterizations in a line, and greater help will be done.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is soft and weak from cold and moisture, so that the patient retenes urine, then do a cauterization in the part below the bladder on the penis, where the hair grows, and one on each side, and make each cauterization as long as our thumb.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and do a cauterization behind, where it was pricked;
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and make the cauterizations pointed according to the form before mentioned.
de la marris	of the mare
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the marital bed is cold and moist, so that it does not promote conception, and the flowers are withered and their time has passed;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, there is great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	then it is necessary that he do three cauterizations in the back, as we have said before for the bladder cauterization, and a cauterization behind.
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and let the cauterization be with nails, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the hip
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the viscous moisture descends into the hip joint box, and for this reason if it moves out of place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and the department of the hip joint is found, so that you cauterize the patient on the hip joint box with the fire cautery in a circular shape, and sign before the place of the hip joint inside the circle as it comes back, so that the box is within the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if be such cauterization as those with which we have cauterized the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if this cauterization is not present, then you shall make three cauterizations of the large olive, and let the cauterization be also perfect as all the others;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat until he is well.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain in the knee
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes to the hip joint, and it is from cold and moisture, and the patient is cured of what we have said in the division, and the treatment does not work, and the disease is old:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	then you must purge the patient of large humors of foul pills, or other bad-looking pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After this, make a fire cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the method of the cautery should be according to two ways:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	that is to say, together burning medicines, and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cautery is according to many ways, of which one is:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	that you cauterize on the hip joint three triangular cauterizations according to this form, and make a deep and large one, and leave a space of two between each cauterization of the thickness of a nut, and let it be olive-colored;
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	yet no times do you make fire cautery in the middle on top of the hip, for there are 4 according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see, if the fire cautery in the ring that we have said before in the dislocation of the hip;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but make it in such a way that the circle contains all the hip, and all the flesh of the leg is burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way it is done in sciatica, when the pain remains in the hip and does not reach the thigh or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it comes only up to the thigh and leg, then make 2 cauterizations at the place where the patient says the pain stays, and 3 above the ankle IV times on the left side a little.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let the cauterization be with the knife, and let the flesh of the leg be burned;
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the patient feels that the pain extends to two or three toes or near them, then cauterize at the place where the pain is felt 3 times or 4 times with the "point" cautery.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if one practices it, one does it well.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if one knows that the pain is in the knee joint towards the thigh, then one does a cut with a surgical knife or a circular one, and you give him good care in all your cauterizations so that you do not leave it there so much as the cautery burns the nerves and large arteries, and so that you do not cause the patient great pain and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I have seen many who have done a cauterization on the heel of the foot and left it so long that the leg went completely limp, and the toes as well, and became pierced and corrupted all the toes.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a solution of the belly which he had, he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two places together, do a cauterization on each one, according to this way.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise people say in the cauterization of the knee joint, how it should be done, do it like this and make it as thick as a knuckle or a little less, and put it between the joints and between each joint there is a quantity of space the size of a pea;
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and the joints are covered on both sides, and they are also like knuckles, and there is good iron in all;
et c’est li forme:	and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	and be heated until it is all red and hot, and then put it on the chest of the sick person, and turn it on his left side;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and cauterize once more, and let it rest for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then make an ointment of butter, and leave the open wound long;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the treatment with ointment until it is well.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasis says that we use little of this cautery because of the doubt of its effectiveness, and those who use it are few;
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and however this is a good cautery, which can bear it, and where it afflicts;
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The medical cautery of burning medicine should be made in such a way that the instrument between the margin of the opening and is of brass or iron on one side, and has two sides, with the quantity of its thickness being half an inch;
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and are at the back and above, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After putting the chest of the horse lying on its back on its belly, and holding your hand very much above the chest of the horse;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After putting the [horse] between the two circles of hot wax that are heated on the fire, and leaving it for an hour in order to suffer the heat and burning of the horse;
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For it has tried the medication as well as fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	And when the medication is over, let your hand with the instrument and raise the horse's belly of soft wax, and leave it thus for three days, and put on cow dung as much as that which is black from the scorching is removed;
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and let him rest for three days so that infection does not enter;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	And this would be behind aid after the cure of onions until it is healthy.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain extends only to the thigh or only to the leg, then make the instrument that you hold according to what you have done in the hip increase.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And this is the way of the hot awes, and I have written it or the treatment of the correction of medicines.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkaline and live chisel, as much of one as of the other, and grind them together, and put them in a nine pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	or there is a small hole that the point of a razor can enter;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and place another well-filled pot on it and put vinegar and soft water on it, until there are two pots of powder that you have well mixed with your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and leave it in this way until there is only water and soil left, then take all the water, and put it on vinegar and soft water as before;
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And so if it is moistened and is made peaceful with the use of medicinal remedies and other cauterizations.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it performs such work as fire, and if with other medicines, which well cauterize the meat as these, and honey of almonds and chalts with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Gallien us tells a cure wherein one honourable was cured of the pain in the hip and sciatic vein, and he made much murmur, and said that another cure was not done, and that he was healed all at once when this cure was made, and he bathed himself as it is taught hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And said in this manner that you grind the green and dry tallow, and pound it with a little fat, and put it on the meat and on the thigh and leg where the pain is, and let it rest;
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and leaves it for three hours and by that quantity that the patient does not feel the burning anymore.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then let him enter or bath as long as his body is a little aroused, and let him enter the bed, and the pain will go away all and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use fire cautery of such medicines, unless after the evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dichoriades says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat hair, it helps a lot;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and this cauterization must be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take another and burn it with oil, and put it on the pit that is between the thumb of the foot and the other which is called the fistula.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After taking the dry hair, and putting it on fire until it turns into coal, and placing it on the wool, and leaving it until it is burned.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and repeat this again, and do not cease to do so as long as you think that it comes up to the hip, and that the pain has stopped;
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and the way of treating with fire is called "cauterization with hair".
de la dolor dou dos	from the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, or from چرور، یا توسط ضربه یا از طریق تخلیه زیاد، یا از شباهت ماده ی سرد گسترش یافته، هیچ یک از این شباهت ها ارزش cauteering ندارند، مگر اینکه آنهایی که از infusions of cold material come.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is appropriate that after the patient has voided bad or similar fluids, a fire be applied to his back where the pain is, three lines of five cauterizations each, and according to the strength and quantity that the sick person can endure;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and the cauterization be done according to the cauterization that is called "the touch";
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see, make three or four cauterizations with the claw-shaped cautery according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	Several times this disease comes to small children, and the signs of the beginning are that he has a tight spine when he stands up and is afraid.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you find in the back spine of the two and in us the appearance that comes on the others.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this person and you see him heal, if he is cauterized with the cautery of that one according to this form:
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the fire cautery is equally applied to each part of the spine.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, so cauterize inside the spine with the piercing cautery two lines or three, and let the punctures be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	Afterwards, heal the area as much as it is healthy according to what we have said, and beware that you do not apply cautery in gibbosity which is in the spice of nerves.
de la dolor des jointes	of the joints' pain
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When the joints hurt from moisture that spread to each limb of the body, and when pain comes in pieces, that mirage is called "rheumatism" properly, and when it is caused by cold and medicines do not cure it, it is cured by cauterization in this way:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	make the cauterization enter into the joint of the foot, and let the cauterization be olive oil according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if it is necessary for you to hold the foot, then make a fire cautery with all the fire cauteries that are claimed "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come up to the knees and to other joints, and this happens many times, let him make a cauterization on each knee three cauterizations or four of each part, all with olive cauterization;
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	and if you have more work to do, but don't hold your hand too hard so that the skin doesn't get burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains go down to the knees and back, administer the cauterization that we have spoken about in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, do not make them too small;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if there is still some pain, but don't go up to each joint and the hair of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if the pains come just as the cuts or just as the shoulders, then cauterize each part and give good government to the patient and apply medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you do this with good government and you purge the fluid, then you will be healed by God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the sutra
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When the rupture comes in the armpit, and the ball falls down to the crotch and is a new injury, then you must first clean it so that it does not get worse.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and he should use things that dry up his belly, so that the end comes from his belly.
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	After that, he should sit down with his back between your hands, and order him to comb his hair as long as the burning feels, and then bring it to your sides, and sign at the base of the fracture on the bone with the fingernail, and mark everything that is like half a circle above the neck;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then heat the fire cautery so that it is ready:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	as long as it is white and it pours drops.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then bring the balls to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and the ministers comb his hair on his back so that it does not turn around;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and work well on the patient's legs, and put a cloth and an iron on his legs, and another one on his hands that comb them;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	Then put the fire cautery on all your hand, and hold it steady and keep holding it until you reach the bone, and if you don't reach it the first time, try again a few times until you do;
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and guard well so that the fire does not splash when you are making the cautery.
que tu ne le brulasses;	that you do not burn it.
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and that through this the patient does not die, or some other misfortune befalls him.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you come to the bone with the cautery, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that the cauterization of children be subtle according to their measure, and of adult people also great according to their measure;
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days treat with fire as much as the scar is healed;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	after the fire treatment apply other remedies until he is well, and place the patient on his back for ten days until the wound has properly healed;
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and it is necessary that his movements be limited for a long time, so that the fire does not splash when he goes to bed.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after ten days, when he wants to get up, let him be given a well-made bandage, and leave it on for another ten days;
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and he should have good rest, so that he works little and wards off too much drinking and eating, and too much pride.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when he has taught this instruction let him be entirely well.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say here after the cure of the cutter in his paste.
de la routure dou ventre	from the rupture of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When the ruptures come in other bellies and are connected, and you see that they no longer grow, then you do the cauterization of cauterization according to its quantity, and burn the third of the wound;
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after the cure according to what we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and none of the above said that it must be cauterized at the cautery of III angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but the first sign is the place of incision and make a line across the width above the rupture, and another below it, and with your hand press all the fire-cauterized part.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterizations are lighter and gentler.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any member
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain arises in any member, or from a knock or a wound, and this pain persists for a long time, and medicine does not help, then it is necessary that he be cauterized with the cauldron which is called 'poins', and the cauterization according to the length of the limb, its smallness, its weakness, its virtue, and its location from twists, and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	if he is well after the first cauterization, it is good;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	this name, restart another cauterization above that one, for such is the custom that he must be moved at the member that is closest to him, so that you do the cauterizations until the patient is well.
de meselerie	of mischief
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The misfortunes are alleviated by cauldron in no way or to a great degree, and most often the disease comes from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	If you see the patient at the beginning, take care that the disease does not spread according to what we have said in the division, and do not let it stop or delay, and if you doubt that corruption will stain the whole body, then make five cauterizations on his head.
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	I cut off his hair at the top of his head, and the other towards the end of his hair by the forehead.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and II behind the two horns, and I behind the hairline;
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and I leave it so much up to the hand that the cauterization comes down to the bone, and so much that the scorches come out without that the vapors of the heavy humors can come out;
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and cauterize over the wound according to what it is in front of you.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if he has a fever throughout;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and let him be obviously burned, if it is necessary that you cauterize them with these cauterys which we have said at the head, and one cautery in his neck, and two cauterys on his spine of the back, and one great cautery on the skull, and one other small cautery, and two cauterys on his shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and two cauterys on the knuckles, and two cauterys on the bones of his hands, and one cautery on each joint of the hands and feet, and cauterys on the palm of the hand;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and beware of the nerves that are under the foot when walking, so that you do not burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	or one cautery on the bone of the hand, and one other on the bone of the stomach, and one on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that when I make more cauterization, I also give more aid, and it brings more benefit;
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	and knows that the patient does not feel any pain at the fire, as those who are well do, for this reason the body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cauterization be great and small according to the limbs and joints, according to what you will find in the way of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	Afterwards, cure with flour of times with honey and other cures as long as he is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When a member swells up and is treated with medicine, oil, and poultices, and is not yet healed, then you make cauterization on the member according to its size and smallness.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and let the cauterization be a little bit inside the flesh of the cure;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then the cure of onions until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And never does one make cauterization by hand and foot and back, at the outlet of the nerve that paralyzes the member, and so if it is broken;
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and do not get in the way of them at all unless one knows the members and outlets of the moving nerves of the body.
de albaras	of armor
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "albaras" is awake, and the medicine's power is nothing, then fire cautery with a single perfect cautery according to the amount of the specific remedy until the blushing is removed, and its color is moved.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	then heal with flour of vetchies and lentils with oil of rose and leaves of plantain, and blood of cock and blood of thrush, each a part;
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	and mix them all together, and bind it with a bandage, and apply it to the affected area until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The cure for leprosy by cauterization:
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the leprosy comes at the beginning, and you see it stop, if the cautery is made with a fire cauldron that seems like a circle, all around the edge of the leprosy.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And all these things say that fire cautery should also be done in the middle of the wound;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	and all this does not seem good to me, because I am afraid that it will become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have never done it once;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and the most right thing is that he be cauterized inside, with the cautery which is called "circule", as we have said in many cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has a disease that is called "adubelati", and it delays death or because of the waste that it makes or because of the age of the sick person when he is very old and has little blood, or because of the heat;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you see him hastening to die:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	then you cauterize him inside with small cauteries by piercing;
aprés le laisse ensi.	Afterwards leave it like this.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see that the whole body is being poked with fire, then heat the fire of this form:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And put your hand in the middle of the disease called "adubelati" as long as the fire has pierced the pulse, and make such fires that the patient feels heat in some way so that the course of corruption is slowed.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After treatment as long as he is perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The fire cure
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another form of disease that is called "corrosion," and is nothing other than a member's putrefaction, for it gnaws away at the members just as dry fire eats away at dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in a person who can suffer the cautery together with fire, then heat the small and large cauteries as much as is suitable for the place or the sick person;
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	Afterwards cauterize all around until you remove all corruption, and nothing remains of it, that all the corrupted part is taken away.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave it for three days, and put oil on the incisions that are hurting from the heat until the burns from the fire have healed over, and all corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of onions causing fever.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see after three days that no sound hair grows, it is good.
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if not, then begin the fire cautery on those that are delayed in their place腐敗。
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this menthol is never once cured with medicine awash instead of fire cautery;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but nonetheless the fire cautery is of greater aid, and I have already said that the cure for the awash medicine is in dislocation:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take it when you need it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of onions that come to toes
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	times have passed that the feet by accidents give birth to a disease which is called "clos" according to our intention, and it is a large, troublesome thing that breaks the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauterization of this disease is in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is to be understood cauterization by fire, and cauterization by hot water.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cautery if you need to heat it up as well, just like a pen of a vault, and let it be made of good iron to the measure that it can drive the nail from all sides, and that it has subtle margins;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	Then put all heat on the nail, and turn your hand totally around the nail as far as it comes to the nail's tip;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and let it remain for three days until it begins to go away;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	then make a poultice of wild rose leaves crushed with sand, and leave the poultice on all night, and tie it tightly and let it root out its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then heal the wound by dressing it every day until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they have been converted by the use of cold, and often come out and into the mouth and the teeth, then you must bring them fire cautery.
et est en teil maniere:	Here is one way to do it:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	Take a twig of argan or iron, or a feather of swallow, and put on the nail and the antelope horn, that is to say, for warts;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	and put the twig on so that it burns all around, then put a little hot water on, and hold your hand firmly, and press your hand turning so that the edge of the twig comes to the root of the nail, and may find the hot water path deep down to the root;
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and suffer the illness a little of the hot water an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	then leave it so, and it will all come out at its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	And so do another one, until you have drained all those who are in the heart, then cure the wounds that cause fury.
li cure dou trembler	the cure of trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When someone shivers from cold or fever or another illness, so that you have to make three or four cauterizations on the spine of the back, one cauterization between each spine;
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and a cauterization on the legs, and one on the stomach with olive oil cauterization;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	will let the shivering stop, and will hasten the healing from the cold illness.
des pustules puans	the pustules that swell
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Once the skin breaks out in pustules that come from corrupt matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	if it seems opportune to the first when they appear that one make a cauterization on each head of the pimple:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	a subtle cauterization with mistletoe bark, so that the tip is taken from the fire, or with the root of a long-hair plant, or with the lentean cauterization.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And once the fire cautery has begun, according to this method, they cannot grow hair in advance, but their excesses are disrupted and they are healed;
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut off
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Many times there are great disturbances of blood from the artery that is cut to the wound, which enters the skin, or from the fire cautery of the limb, and similar things;
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is a very painful thing to stop breathing.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And wherever there is an opening, if you quickly put your little finger on the wound of a vein, and strain it as much as the pain subsides from your little finger, and no more drops come out;
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	then place fire cauterization olive oil on many small and large ones until they are all red;
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	and then take, or a big or small according to the wound and its place where the artery is cut, and put the cautery on that vein where you hold your two, and keep the cautery there until the blood stops flowing.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if he seizes a fire when you feel your second pain in the vein, and the cautery is finished, if you take another cautery that are on fire quickly.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not cease to do this one after the other until the blood has stopped flowing;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and beware that you do not burn the nerve which is delicate, and that no other evil comes upon the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and know that when the blood stops flowing from the artery, it cannot be stopped well even if the artery is large, unless one of the four ways we have mentioned:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	by cautery, by extraction when it has not been treated, by a very tight thread, or by medicines placed on it which have the power to stop the flow of blood;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And let him lie and be restrained with a bandage.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will administer a tight bandage or place burning things on it, or similar things, if it does not benefit, then do not do it.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	If this happens to anyone and he has neither sight nor medicine ready, then he should put his index finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and firmly tighten it onto both the wound and the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and don't move the finger, but rather cool it often with cold water until the blood is frozen and thick and hardened.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And make questions of those who are skilled in cauterizing and medicine.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of cures for diseases related to the body's joints and muscles.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you about the first chapter, in which all diseases are treated with fire, hot medicines, and the needling and causes and instruments and forms of cauterization.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	And I have put this chapister on the top of the shoulder, and I will go into this chapister by that middle way for those who ache more lightly than those who ache more painfully.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so, since I have begun to speak of this, it is necessary that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first chapter of the cauterizations, and therefore greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you that you do not undertake madness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For in this way people come to their end.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	if they come from those who have such a disease that they die easily due to the hardship of their disease, and the great severity of their illness;
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	and from which one must be afraid.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And from these I have a message for you, and he says:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am old.
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the illness is contemptible.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	It only concerns you to consent to those who come to you and have this way, but put more great confidence in your honor than in your own interest, and do not open it carelessly but carefully from him of whom you are certain, and from whom you could have taken it and kept it;
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	and use prediction and indication in the treatment of your patients so that health is converted.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	this will help you achieve a good reputation, glory, and memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, Our Lords grant you good understanding and justice, and if you will ask for the holy inspiration of His hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have ordered this chapter in devising by chapters, according to the one that is before or the chapter of the cauterization, which I have devised from the chief to the tip, so that you may find more easily that of which you will have need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	dou chief plein d’aigue
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	You know that this disease often comes to infants from excessive suckling, and when the child babbles too much, it strains the baby's head.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	and never does this come from the cause of a repugnance that is known.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this disease affect anyone but children, and all those who have had it die quickly;
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	and for as much as it seems to me that I must be more careful in using this treatment in the future.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw a child whose shoulders were weak and whose head would fall over every day until it could not be supported.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and this moisture caused his death, and this moisture so joins the bones together over his skull, between the cheek and the bone;
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and if they are so large that the moisture is between the tendon and the bone, and the tendons are small, then you should cut a wide slit with your knife at the top of the leg.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and as far as we know, until the moisture runs.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and give it this form of a spaulder:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is deeper, and the abscess larger, then make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	and if the moisture is out of the bone, and the signs that you see are the combs of the leg overspread on each side, and the liquid jumps up sharply when you press it with your hand towards the inside, and it does not respond to you:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	then you should cut a slit in the leg according to this method:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all the moisture completely.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After having closed the slits with cloths and powders, and have put wine and oil on them, and left them like that for five days;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	then remove the cloths and powders, and clean the wound with patches and oil, and let the head hang freely, and feed the patient with meat that is dry enough so that the member heals and is healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another way of cutting is that you look at where the aperture of the abscess is large, and the gathering of the fluid.
car aucune fois est elle devant;	For it is never before;
aucune fois derrier;	behind
aucune fois en destre;	on the right
et aucune fois en senestre.	and on the left
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	so cut where the abscess opens, and the draining of the fluid, and do it according to what you are able to do;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and guard that you do not block the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and bring a flow of blood, so that the patient dies from a loss of blood and an evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of remedy
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When there is a disease that is called "cough" or "pit", and the disease is old, and the remedy of medicines does not benefit, then the following remedy should be used: cauterize with what you will cover the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is therefore necessary, since you cannot block the views, for the patient to raise his head;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	afterwards rub the place with a rough cloth until the arteries open, and then extract the patient's neck from all the cloth;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	and see where the vein is pulsing, and its lobes on either side are after the ears, and they are closed;
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then mark the lobes of the cheek, then cut each on either side with a scalpeling blade from two parts, as far as the tooth, and this one be done by the broad edge of the blade.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see, remove the spatula from the artery and cover it on top, cutting as well as II do on the back.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is covered, let it continue to rise continually without stopping.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not open to the sense, then you must measure the quantity of the space of three fingers, then mark the cheek and cut it up to the bone;
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and this one, which concerns the blood to be removed, is six parts, and by chance a little more or less, according to what the patient can suffer, and the regrowth of the artery;
puis regarde la plaie:	then look at the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	if it remains on the bone point of pain, if the scalpeling of the abscesses does not come out, then extract the wound and bind it, and the treatment of pus as long as it is healed.
de emigrainne	of grinding
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When the ancient grindstone comes and catarrh is acquired due to moisture in the temples and old scabs and similar things, and it is treated by the methods of medicinal remedies and all that does not benefit him, let us extract the arteries from the temples and cauterize them, as we have told.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the way of extracting them is that the patient should make his hair grow again on his temples, and listen to the artery which opens in the temple, for it opens well by its beating, and is little seen but in some men who are too cold;
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	and if it is seen, then the patient should remove his clothes from some sheets, and then rub the place with no rough cloth, and raise the place with hot water until the artery appears clearly;
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the spasmodic mass where this is the shape:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then peel the skin lightly until you come to the artery, then tie it up with pinches, and remove well the webs that are attached to each part;
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	and if the artery is thin, then turn it with the point of the hook, and cut off that part according to the quantity of the two chapters.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut, then nothing will remain whole or intact.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And there are six chapters of this book, until three.
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	and if the artery is large, you should tie it in two threads of strong silk, so that blood does not come out before the wound heals, and comes out gradually.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	then cut the excess between the two threads at that moment too, and then, if you see it, with fire cautery from the cut edge as far as the bone is cut;
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	and this is the operation, if the patient does not have a fever and has a warm complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For cauterizing is done to end the moisture:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	for this is more powerful against moisture.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	Or it is necessary for the extraction of arteries to fill the space with fine cotton and put it on well-made bandages;
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and when they are dislocated, if one is cured with dry medicines that cause a التشنج، and tents, until they are healthy؛
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	and if you do not cut the artery as much as you can do it, if you hurry to cover it with fire, or employ lead vitriol and extract it from your hand so that the blood does not flow؛
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	and if you do not have it present, if you place your finger on the ice-cold water as long as the blood does not flow, and raise the head of the ice-cold water until the blood stops, and is extracted as it should be؛
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	and that which is swollen and lighter in extraction from the artery is that you cauterize the edge of this fire from both sides, but let the cutting be very slow so that it lasts longer on the heat.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instrument is too soft, if it retains its heat less.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	And it should have between the two knives a space of a thumb wide, and then when you have cut through both sides, and you take off a little with the sharp edge, then cut into the bone with fire as much as it comes out, and cover the wound in two places؛
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	and are separated between the two shoulders, for it is not joined to this fire cautery from head to toe.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	and this is the form of the cautery:
des larmes	tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When the tears of the eyes flow down from a vein that is above the temple at the top of the head, and does not benefit from any medicine that is made, and you see the face of the patient grow pale, and feels a tingling sensation as if it were freezing;
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	and the oil is thin and moist so that the hair of the scalp falls out, and the scalp is burned and scalded by the heat of the tears, then it is necessary for this treatment.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	And they called it the 'old treatment', and that is what you do for the patient who has this condition in his hair on his forehead, then make three incisions at equal intervals along the length of his forehead;
