And when all the bowels that are in the abscess are emptied, then fill the wound with cotton, and leave it until the next day, then remove all the cotton, and treat with ointment from now on until it is healed.
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.	And if the abscess is like scrofula, then cut it as we have said in cutting scrofula, and if there is pus in the wound, then apply fire cautery as we have said before.
de la routure de l’artere	of the rupture of the artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	When the artery is torn and the flesh that covers it is torn too, then often an abscess forms, and in the same way the wound escapes into the abscess.
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	And if we cut into it as soon as the artery is exposed, then the abscess will be completely filled;
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	and when you feel it on both sides, if you feel extraction;
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	and when it is for the vein, then let it be cut away carefully;
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	It is madness to cauterize this abscess, and most certainly when it is cut open and the flesh torn and the blood comes out, and it is full of worms and maggots, and very great.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	Therefore it is necessary to avoid cauterizing with iron, and the one that is at the head must also be avoided, and in that which is swollen with an artery, cut the skin from above;
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	then work on the abdomen like a single cloth, and separate the artery from the veins as much as it is uncovered.
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	then stick a pin in it, and let it pierce to the other side, and pull out the artery with a double thread of two strands, according to what I have taught you about the extraction of the two arteries that are in the temples;
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	then point out the line that is between the two links of an intramuscular injection as far as there is no hair on it, and take off the abscess;
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	then bring about the cure that I have just mentioned, until the thread chatters;
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and treat this with oil coming from this, until it is healthy;
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	and the abscess is to be opened by the vein, if it is convenient that you hold with your hand what you can of the abscess on all the skin, then stick in the pin at the line that you hold in your hand, and let it pierce with a double thread, so that you pull it out from the other side;
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	and then join the aperture, as I have told you, with thread from one of the two sides to the shoulder blades;
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	and if you doubt that the thread will not hold fast, if you run another needle through all the thread from one end to the other of the incision made by the first needle, and then pull the thread in four lengths;
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	and then cut away the excess as it comes free from the incision, and then cut away the remaining thread and leave the one that is tied;
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then put wet cloth on it with wine and oil, and then give him treatments of herbs and spices until he is well.
des apostemes des ners	of the nerves of the neck
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	So too do the nerves come from the artery and the vein, they come to the nerves when they are torn, or by too much work, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	And when it comes to the shoulder joints and the two sides of the body where they are joined together, this is a sign of trouble, and its color is like the color of the chest, and it is in many states without pain.
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	and when they are restrained, if the patient feels pain, and is not perfectly cured of the course, but delay treatment;
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	and mute well on all sides, and do not go forward or backward, nor above nor below, and the one who is in joints does not come together with iron:
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	for fear of a contraction;
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	and those who are at the head or at the front, make the skin with the spatulate.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	If the abscess is small, if it has a nail in it, and cut it at its root;
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if it is large, if the nail is in the onion, and scorch it, then break the bone and join the wound by stitchwork, and cure as long as it is healed.
des grosses boces pendans	the large bellies hanging down
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	Now there comes a disease in the belly and not elsewhere, which is called "mould" by its appearance, and the root is subtle, and the head is big;
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	and if they are small and large.
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	and I saw some that had two bellies that were more like fungi than anything else, and there was no difference between them, and they were white, and they had small roots, and they were cut in half, and ran together with moisture.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I picked them up and found one to weigh XVIII ounces, and the other VI з., and in the incision of the ovary so that you look at it the patient is moist, and the color of the arteau is white and moist and has a thin root;
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	if it is coped with a large spatule, and let the cautery be in the fire.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	For at the tailor there are often too great movements of blood, and it escapes from you, so hurry up then the cauterizer.
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	and if you see the patient dying and frightened by the incision of the iron, then take a well-made thread of pluck, and bind the arteau as we have said, and leave it for II days;
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	and then the restraint, and do not cease to strip the thread of linseed as long as it copes with the arête, and sometimes through it work.
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	and if the roots are large, so as not to hurt him with a chopper in the middle for the belly, but you can well chop half of it, then cauterize that he does not return.
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	then heal the wound, and make sure you do not chop off the tuft that is of bad color and poor taste and milk regart.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For this is an abscess with a crust, and I will come to treat the leprosy which follows.
quant li boude ist fuer	When the wound is healed
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	If the appearance of a bulge comes out by fire or cut on a wound or split, and is on the belly and there are some of the bulges, as it would be in other cuts, or blood that cuts off a vein or an artery according to what is before, or windiness;
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	and if it is by the cut of the syphus and by the issue of the bulge, if the color of the abscess is similar to the color of the flesh, and it is a light thing without pain, and opening of different issues.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is because of the issue of the intestine, then it is more varied, and when one presses it towards his two legs so that it returns, and then comes back again, and perhaps if it is stuck, and enlarges much at the entrance to the basin and by strong work.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	And if it's due to moisture, it's a light thing, and open well when you press it with your hand, do not constrain at all;
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	and if it's due to blood, if open by these signs the large and hard abscess, and is poked according to a quantity;
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	and if it' s due to wind, if there is a sound at the buttocks, and the opening is that you look at its appearance it' s for blood of the artery, or vein, or wind.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	If you should leave the cure.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For there is doubt and fear, as I have told you before, or chapistle abscesses, for the artery and for the vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	And if the appearance is for the intestine or the bowel, then it is appropriate that you instruct the patient to wet his anus, and be extended all straight, then sign of touch all around the bowels;

puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	and the body wrapped with a strong thread or a cord of strong silk tightly, and let us bind him.
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	Then operate on half the abscess stretched out on the thread, and insert your index finger, and feel the intestine.
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	If you find that he is caught in the thread, then release him, and insert the intestine at the bottom of the abdomen.
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	And if you find the boil, then take it with a lance, and cut off the excess.
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	And if the artery is opposed or blocked, then make a loud noise inside, then return to your operation and take two needles, and insert two threads, and insert the two needles where you made the hole that you made pierce;
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	Then stretch the abscess in four places on the needles, and if you see, remove the needles, and leave it to putrefy for as long as possible, and cut off the flesh by itself.
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	and then you make the incision when it is soft and porous, then heal it as we have said;
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	and extract the blood or moisture that you find, then heal the joint of what it corresponds to, and bind the joint.
dou chancre	Of the sore of the leg
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	We have said in the division the appearances of cancer, and how it must be operated with medicines, and how one should treat the cure with iron;
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	and let us say that the cancer is removed from the breast, and great caution in its cure, and the old man said that when cancer is in a place where it can be cut off as cancer in milk, and in the cuisse, and in similar places, and it must all be cut off when it is in the beginning;
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	and when it is large and old, then you must not approach it, for I have never found anything healthier;
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	There was never one like this before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	And the incisions, when they are in place or can be removed, as we have said, are that you purge the black blood never once.
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	then make him well if he has manifest fullness, then done the incision I good place to do the work;
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	then pour your scalpel or ulcer, and the hair of all parts, and the bone of all parts leave nothing;

puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then the doctor treats other diseases as long as he is healthy.
de ydropisie	about dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	We have said in the division the appearances of hydropsis, and in what way the accumulation of water is made, and the signs of each appearance, and the treatment that is done with medicine, and that which is cured with iron:
si est eclites soulement;	If it is dislocated only.
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	and one must not touch metal in these two cases:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	that is to say, tympany and hypostasy, for it is a deadly thing;
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	so when you treat this condition of dropsy, which is called "eclites", with medicines, and the cure does not benefit, if the patient is weak, or if he has another disease besides dropsy, such as a stomach complaint and similar things;
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	if one does not touch metal, for there is doubt;
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	and if you see the patient of great vigor, and he has no other disease but dropsy only, and he is not too old or too young, then thus should you act:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	lay the patient down directly on your hands, and press the abdomen in toward the lower part of the spine, then take the spatulum with thorns according to this form:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	and cut into two parts.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	a point, and all ways not be so intren that he can come jusc' to the intestine when one puts it in, and cannot bruise him;
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	and then look if there is water retention inside the abdomen:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	if it comes out straight from the buttock, three fingers right below the hip bone;
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	and if there is water retention due to liver disease, then your incision on the left side of the hip bone;
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	and if it is due to pus, then on the right, and it is not necessary that the patient lie down on his back so that the excess does not run into the weak part;
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	then pierce all the skin with the instrument, and cut it, and hold your hand to all the skin between the skin and the sfac as much as you can with your thumb or index finger; like peeling an onion;
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	and then pierce the loz with so much pressure that the liquid comes out from within, and this is the source of the pain; then treat it more forcefully, and pour this instrument into which this form is found.
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it looks like a silver knife that is very thin, and it is made of bronze or copper that is very light, and there is a small hole in its center.
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	and one end is sharpened, and there is a small hole.
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	and one end is blunt, and the other is sharp.
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	and the head is cut off so that it resembles a feather, and this is the shape of the incision that the scribes cut with their quills:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	at the top of the instrument, so that when the liquid comes out, it drips onto the instrument.
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	empty it halfway or a third of it, because if you empty more than that at this time, perhaps the patient will die from the loss of his spirit due to the weapon's impact, or he will faint or approach death.
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	but according to the quantity of its virtue, and according to what the dispositions of the virtue of the disease mean, and its hairs;
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	then train the instrument and hold back the water, and it is held back now by the curve that stops the perforation which is on the side, of which I have spoken, that you pierce according to this way;
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	then begin again with the instrument another day, if you see the patient suffering, and train a little quantity of water;
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	do not do it any day, and keep yourself from doing so as long as he does not stay but a little bit of water.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you doubt about the patient, and you leave him with a little water, if the cure of the burial or sand is hot, and by sweating or bathing and in the sun, and if he gets tanned by drinking;
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	and the treatment of drying medicines as long as he is healthy, and cauterizes on the stomach and on the liver and on the spleen after the extraction of the water, as I said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	the constriction of the throat
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	There is no child born who does not have a foreskin, or if the foreskin is small, or if it is not in its place.

et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	and they cannot conceive because the material cannot come out until it reaches the testicles, and this is a bad disease.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	And the way of this treatment is that the patient lies down on his back, then put the head of the penis and the cup up to the size of a feather, so that the piercing goes in the middle, as it should.

des pustules de la verge	of the pustules of the penis

Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	The cauterization should be performed together with these two preparations:

de la circoncision	of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	Circumcision is not a continuous cure if it is like the other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	However, when we do this work of our will, and particularly on infants, it is necessary that we do the best work and the lightest work for salvation.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the old people did not speak about circumcisio of their children, for they do not use it in their law, and we have only obtained this knowledge through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	For I have wanted the greatest part of the masters and the most famous who performed circumcision around the anus, and with force, and all a новакule;
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	since it is the course of this operation that there are two holes, and perhaps if one covers that above and holds that below.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	Or the hand is brought back into place, and the pain doubles, and the purification that comes from the blood is not yet assured at the tip of the limb.
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	And for the purification of the nail, by chance, the wound is lost, and they correct the work, and many times it comes out like this that there is no need for purification and I want it.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	From the purification that is done with force on all the thread I have found the goodness of the experiment, because the forces cut just as much above as below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand, if you cut it evenly all along, then release it.
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	But that the thread is well tied at the end of the skin;
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	and be the manner of the first work so that you make the child think, if he hears it, that you do not tie the thread tightly around the staff, and then make it fall in all ways that you can;
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	then let it rest straight between your hands, and turn the threads between your hands or keep your fingers so that the child does not see them, nor any of the tools;
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	and dip your hand to the root and blow on it, and hold it up as high as the head of the root is;
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	then clean it well with dirt that is gathered there, then tie the joint with a double thread, then cut it to the other side of the thread;
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	and hold it in place with the second thread at the root and middle finger, and cut between the two threads, then blow on it from above the hospital and hold the head of the root;
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	then let the blood run a little bit at a time, because that is what causes the bleeding;
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and put powder on top of the powder that is made with a mixture of cooked oil and water, and cover it with a cloth, leave it there overnight, and have another doctor treat him until he gets better;
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The form of force for purifying if this is:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The two heads should be soft and pliable, and the heads themselves should also be as long as possible and evenly shaped.
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	For the mistake of purification if when the curative fluid escapes through incisions:
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	Then it is necessary that you stretch it out with your hand so that the veins form an abscess.
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	And make it even, and if you cannot hold it with your hand, then hold it with tongs, and then make it even.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if it has passed three days, and that which is sore at the root is swollen, let it remain until the abscess has become calm, and then scrape it lightly.
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	If you can move it as you wish, and keep the part of the root away from it, that will not harm it.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Cure therefore the powder from things that cause a wound, which we have said is to be used in the treatment of powders, and if it is applied in excess, and it goes up, it will not hurt.
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Cure therefore, as we have said, as long as it is well.
dou retenement de l’urine	how to retain urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is due to the operation of a stone, or frozen blood, or bowels, or similar things, which we have mentioned in the division;
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	and if the urine does not flow freely, and you see an obstruction due to a stone in the bladder or at the neck of the bladder, then it is fitting that the patient should be bent on his knees;
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	and let him lie on his back, and extend his stomach from the upper part of the back, and restrain the patient so that he lies down as much as he can;
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	and therefore the collar of the bladder is forced to express the stone above, so that the urine is discharged;
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come, as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must use all the instruments that are called "syringe", because this is the form:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	and be of fine light silver, as the feathers of an owl;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	and be of the length of a palm and a half, and be thin at the tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And the manner of issuing urine is that you take a double thread, and tie it to the tip with a piece of wool or cotton, and dip the tip into the syringe;
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	and fill the superfluity of the wool and dip it to the tip of the syringe, then oil the syringe with oil or butter and astringent of mint, and make the patient sit on a chair, and oile the bladder and the penis with moist oil and olive oil and water;
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	Then lightly place the syringe on the penis, until it reaches the base of the penis, then double the penis over towards the testicles.
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	Then draw back the syringe up to the bladder, and let the patient feel for the hollow spot, and this should not be done without following these instructions, otherwise he who guides it or wherever it goes will be twisted.
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	Then tie the string around all of the hair tightly, and let the urine flow through the hair, then remove it forcefully, and make the urine run.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	and start over with the syringe as the bladder is empty, and let the patient lie still.
des maladies de la vessie	of the diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When blisters or sores come to the bladder, or it is infected, and you see water and medicine distilling there, so do all the instruments that are called "clepsydras", and this is their form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It is closed, and if at three openings:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	On one side, and on the other, as you see it;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	And let the hair fall so that the medicine falls correctly on the penis without a trace, and if one can draw out the moisture, and squeeze it when needed.
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	and when you see your medicines move in the bladder, put the head of the patient on a wet cloth, and treat while moving along who is there;
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	if you will treat the moist by the head, and then turn it hard forward who is there;
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	if the moistures enter in, and come to the bladder now, so that the patient will feel them;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	and this is the form of the subtle کلستر which we use to clister the bladder:
si est ci:	if so:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	And it is silver or copper, and the head is higher;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	and desalt at the root or the linden tree;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	Then take a sheep's bladder and put the moisture that you see to clisterize the bladder, then tie it between the two breasts formed of a good doubled thread, and heat the moisture over the fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	put the head of the pis in the penis, then pull your hand over the bladder toward the moisture coming forward until the patient feels that this moisture has come to the bladder.
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	if you don't have a bladder, take a piece of parchment, and make it into a circle, and pierce it roundly around.
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	then pour a strong thread into these holes, then join the circle as one joins a cloth, and put inside what you want of oil and moisture and water, and tie it in the instrument;
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	and do so as you did with the bladder, squeeze your hand until this moisture comes to the bladder.
de la piere	from stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have already said in the division the ways of stone, and extraction together medicines;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	and I have said the difference between the stone that is inside as rain, and all signs, and how one must work with size in stone;
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	and in the bladder, and in the penis.
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	and I will tell you openly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that the stone in the bladder, if it happens more often in children, is a sign that the water leaps from the bladder, similar to water in its subtlety.
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	and I open her again, and I wipe the patient's penis, and I rub it many times, and then it becomes smooth again;
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	and at the root of these jumps the foundation;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and it is light for the cure of children until they are four years old, and much heavier in the elderly, and there is much pain at mid-life, and with the young and the old.
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	and it is lighter to heal those who have large stones than those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, if it is necessary first to purify the patient with a enema, in order to draw out all the matter that is in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it is not often necessary to seek the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by the feet, and move him downwardly while turning him, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and does not jump from one side to the other.
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	and place it between your hands, and his hands shall be down on his thighs so that the bladder is completely downhill;
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	then look and touch inside;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	if you feel the stone in space, so hurry to cut on top of the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not seem right to you when you feel the stone in space, so moisturize your little finger with oil from your left hand, if the disease is hard, or your second finger, if the disease is juvenile and accomplished;
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	and pour it into its foundation, and look at the stone, and when you feel it with your index, if the pain is in the neck of the bladder;
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	then press on top of your index, and pour it toward where you see cutting.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And command the minister to press the bladder toward his hand, and command him to extend his right hand with the arteries up, and with his left hand grasp the skin that is down on the arteries in the part where the cut is made;
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	And I dip the spatula, so that this is its shape:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And place between what is between the hip bones and the base, not in the middle but at the edge of the left side;
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	and let it be on the stone, and your two are close to the base, and let him cut down on it so that it is wide at the bottom, and narrow from above, according to the quantity of the stone, not too big;
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	So that the press may be there where your two are close to the base, so that it does not need work;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	and know that he has stone or angles, and edges:
si est griés a issir;	So it is ready to be cut;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	And if it has stone that is sharp, resembling a gnat, and round, whose edge is light.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	So it will not be hard to cut: And if it has stone that is sharp and round, make the cut larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	and if it does not fall, then you must extract it with the pliers which are like a file on the head, so that the stone is extracted and does not escape.
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	or you take the subtle corbed instrument
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	and if you cannot make it fit, then you open it with a small knife, and if it splits, then extract it with vitriol.
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	and if there is more than one stone, then take the largest first to the collar of the bladder, then chop it down, and then pull it out with force, and the smaller ones afterwards if there are any more.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	If the stone is very large, it is appropriate to make a larger wound.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	either he dies, or his urine comes again through the hole that the water cannot pass through.
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	however you must try to extract it, or with pliers, piece by piece;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	and when you have finished your work, if you employ the incense wound and aloe and dragon's blood, and the strapping, and place over it a damp cloth in oil and wine, or in oil and rose water and cold water to soothe the abscess;
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	then remove the disease from his neck, and do not loosen the ligature until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you have dislocated it, then arise well oil and water its place, then cure it with the ointment of black cumin and with ointment basilicon until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if hot abscesses come into the wound and putrefactions of blood in the bladder, and hold back the urine, which is conveyed in a certain way that it does not run with urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	then put two on the wound, and take out the blood, for if it is left, it will corrode the bladder, and pour it out;
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and raise the wound with water and mud and straw, and help in all ways that you can until it is healed;
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	and it is necessary that all the hours that you cure him, you tie his two legs, and gather the medicines on the place.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small, and it is put down from the penis, and stuck in, and the urine cannot come out;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	if the cure of this which I have thus said, that you cut it many times, is done without excuse from the cutting because of this cure.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have proved this.
Pren I foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a III angles fichiees en I tison:	Take care to forge it according to this form, and be it three inches long, fixed with three pins:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	then take a thread and tie it around the penis above the stone, so that it cannot come back into the bladder;
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	then pour the water lightly on the penis until it comes to the stone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	and turn the file in your hand in the stone point by point, until you can pierce the stone from another side;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	if the urine comes soon, then press your hand on this which is delayed from the stone that is inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	If he is suddenly bruised, and jumps with urine, and gets worse the disease.
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	And if you cannot do this by any means to harm him, then take a wedge of stone and another above it, and push the wedge firmly into the stone between the two lines, and then extract it forcefully, and then loosen the two lines, and clear the frozen blood from the wound.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat him until he is healthy.
de la piere des femmes	from the women's stone
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	It should be noted that a stone can get stuck in a woman, and if it ever gets stuck once, there is great danger to the patient, and it is prevented by three things:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	the first is that perhaps the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	and the second is that one cannot find a woman who is well-versed in midwifery, even if she is married.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third way is that perhaps one cannot find a woman who is knowledgeable about this craft with her hands.
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	and the fourth method is that the stone of the woman is more perfect than the stone of the man, because it requires deeper incision and great fear. And if necessary send to one, you should squeeze a well-learned midwife, and not cut the navel, and if you don't cut it, do not even try to cast subtle mirth;
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	and the present a skilled midwife in the life of women, or a woman who knows a part of the art, and commands her to do what you command in the incision of the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and look well that the woman is virgin;
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	then it is convenient to put out his right hand or fundament and seek the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she cuts it, then bind her right hand, and recommend her to put out her right hand or cup with the malady, and press and press her left hand on the bladder formed.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she pees, then it is necessary that she move from the bladder's entrance to the anus gradually, until she reaches the root of her thigh.
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	Then cut into the stone in the root of the thigh against the middle part where it is muscled, and feel the stone in that part;
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and do not move her two above the stone or anus, and make the cut first small;
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	Then press tightly in the wound, if you feel the stone as much as possible so that it can come out, and know that there are many kinds of stones:
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	That is to say, small and large, sharp and smooth, long and round, and some are rained.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	If you know the appearances so as to know the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the stone does not come out, then put it in vinegar, and keep it for an hour until the stone is taken out.
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	and come back to your work, until the stone is far away, and take the tools that I told you about in the extraction of the stone for men to help you in your work;
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	and if it goes out for you, and this is the artery that has been cut, put the powder on the place and extract it from the bottom and the bend, and do not repeat it, and leave the stone and do not draw it, except by chance the patient dies;
puis cure la plaie.	then heal the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the wound is abated, and the blood clotted, if it returns to your work, as long as the stone is away.
de hernie carnouse	of hernia carnous
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Ramie water is nothing other than assembled moisture or white salt that is the cure for joints, which contains blood.
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	and it is called "syfac", and is not properly in the fabric of the sheep, if one thinks that it is another sheep;
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	and this is the leather of the joint between white salt that we have said;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	and if he does not have it.

de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	It seems to me that it is better to let them grow.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	and I will tell you the treatment and the appearance of an abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say therefore that most abscesses come from within, and least often from outside;
et c’est par mout de cas.	and this is by chance.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	It is known that by acrid and bitter fluid, which increases in the abscess, or by contact;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	And the color of the abscess according to the color of the flesh;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and does not always cause pain, and is an abscess of trouble;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	and sometimes an abscess is grimy and piercing, and of strange color, and never comes from a vein or swelling;
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is from an artery, if you know the position of the abscess, then when you press it with your two fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	and it is not necessary for you to touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	The one made from a vein is known by its disposition to the touch of the two, and can do well in sizing this shape, and other shapes;
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	and is that you take care of the curls of the hair, then is the fur on top, and the thread white well, and deliver the suspension from all sides of the fur.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the fur is already soiled with these new curls, then it is necessary that you take the fur, and the curl;
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	and if it is white again, or in this one that is inside the veils, then it is necessary that you deliver all that is kept, and the curl gently.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the birth of the character is behind the egg, then it is appropriate that you cope all of it, and extract the egg, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is done, if you cover the wound with wool wetted with oil and wine, then he will be cured by other treatments until he is well.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess wrapped in a wrap that resembles a cherry, with the softening of the curls, and the patient grumbles painfully when he goes.

de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the sutra
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The remedies of this chapter are so by the incison that comes or cure, or extension on the belly in the part of the entrails, so that the intestines descend from that incision to one of the balls;
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	and this incision is either by the cure, or by the extension on it, and these two ways come from different causes:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	or by hitting, or jumping, or braying, or by removing pain caused by a similar thing;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	and the signs when it is about the extension of the syrup, if it happens little by little, for a long time, and does not come suddenly;
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the abscesses are even up to the end, lest the syrup rush out.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are when it is due to the section of the sutra, that it brings about a sudden pain, and the apophemis are different in appearance, pressing on the skin, and this is for the exit of the intestine and the body away from the sutura.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And never remove the loops with intestines, and are held back, and cause great pain to the patient, even when it is pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	In these treatments of fear, because it must be avoided.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the technique of opening: order the patient that he keeps the intestine in his hand towards the wound, if it can be pushed back in;

et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and ask your two fingers if there is any hard or white part wrapped in intestine, and if you find nothing, pour into the abdomen.
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	then take a needle that has a thick thread made of ten threads, and dip it in the back part of the scrotum, which is after the skin of the crotch;

de hernie carnouse	of hernia carnous
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this recipe I have never seen anyone dare to make the cure with fire.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancient ones said that it is made as a bundle of reeds which are joined together, in such a way that you tie the vassels, after cutting on one side lightly with a knife;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	Then cut it and heal the abscess of this one who works, as long as the reeds drip;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and heal it as we have said, until he is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	No time comes without a wound between the legs, as we said, and opens the veins.
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and do not draw any of the intestines out with cords, and if they are drawn, it is a little, and he repairs every hour;
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and, moreover, if he stays too long in this place, so that the wound or syphacus believes it, until the intestines are drawn;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and what happens because of the extension of the syphacus that is between the legs, as we said, for it is extended, then it softens and opens the veins and opens them;
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	and the cure if it is by fire, as we have said before;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and no time is cured with iron in this way:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	and it is that the sick person lies still on his back between your hands, then cover the place of the wound with a wide cloth according to the quantity of three days;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	And then take out the leech which is on the skin that is affected, and then take the thread and tie it to the apparent place of the leech;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	And then press him firmly in the belly, and cut the two apparently-present leeches on top of the thread, and cut both of them;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	And then take out the thread's end, and do not cover up the leech nor stretch out any other thing, as I have told you in the treatment of the intestinal ramose;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Then treat it with the treatment of wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you tie up the wounds, if it is a burn, then heal the wound as soon as possible.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The syrup is constrictive, and does not have an appearance in the cut, and the cauterization is wet in this place, and closer to salvation.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of softening the leather of the hips
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Often is the skin of the scrotum softened in some men, so that the worms that are within it are softened, and is to be seen;
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	And it is necessary, when one cures it, that the worm be made to come out onto the skin, and the skin which is softened be placed on top of the natural skin;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	Then join the two lips with a stitch, and cut off the excess skin, soften the leather with three stitches or four firmly.
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	then cover between the seams, and clean as with the other wounds, until it is healed, and cut off the thread.
dou chastrement	Dou cautere de feu comande au malaide qu’il laisse les poilz tant qu’il soient lons et igals; et s’il le poignent a lor nassance, se li estraint les eulz qu’il ne se muevent tant qu’il naissent.
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	I know that chastisements are unbecoming in our law, and for this reason I would not like to speak of them in this book;
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and are necessary only in two ways:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	that one is that the mirror should answer when it is asked, and that its cure be known;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other, because we have often had to chastise some animals for our own benefit, such as rams and sheep and pigs and others.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say that chastisement is done in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	or by attraction, or by cutting.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the one that we do by attraction, let us sit the beast in warm water, until the joint is softened and during;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then dip it in your hand, until they are set and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	Of the cauterization of wounds:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	it is necessary that you hold the beast, and press the skin of the joints to your left hand, then tie the suspender, and cap on each leg as you have well scorched them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and I leave no patch of fat or thin fat that is over the joints;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this method of cauterization is more durable than that which is made by attraction, for in attraction there may be some delay in the joints, because the beast desires lust;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then heal the wound until it is well.
des hermofrodites	Of hermaphrodites: It is fitting that you take the best heifer, and press the skin of the cows to your left hand, then tie the suspensory, and bandage each eye with a bandage, when you have well scorched them; and leave no hole in the splay and the sub-tige which is on the vats; and this mode of chastisement is more mature than that which is done by attraction, for what if attraction may happen that there is no thing of the cows, so that the cow desires luxure; then heal the wound until it is well.
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermaphrodite is one of two kinds:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	one is that between the two cunts it has also like the figure of nature of a woman, or it has hair, and sometimes in the cunt it ejaculates urine.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other way is in women, and it has on the loins knuckle also as a penis and two crotches.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment for man and woman is that you cup the breasts together, and treat them as other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	in the second manner, of men whose urine jumps out through the cunt, if it is not cured.
de la tentigene	of the tentacle
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Tenting is a joint that comes on top of the natural part, until it is too ugly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	and some women also have it great like a hand, and this is the treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	It is necessary that you cut off the surplus of the tenting from your hand or anus, and deal with it lightly;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not cut too much all at once, that the blood does not run too much, and then treat it with another treatment until it is healthy;
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and there is another horse that was not born at the mouth of the mare, and he saddles it, and perhaps he will jump, and it is according to the appearance of a cow, and for this reason they called it the old "cow disease".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If you have to cut it, as we said before, and heal it until it is well.
de erratique	of errant
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	It is error when nature of the woman is not yet perceived, or the hernia is small.
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is natural by birth, or happens by accident that come;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is by horse that it is jostled, or the subtle or secret medicine, and is made perfect in the mare, or at the cost, or at the source, or whatever;
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and they hinder it to conceive, and the delivery, and by chance the flowers to bear.
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and the knowledge of this is through the motion of the balls.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	For if the stoop is close at hand, appearing suddenly, would you like it to be towards your two hands or to the right?
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is subtle medicine, and it is near to books, if you hurry, and turn quickly:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	Hold both of your fingers together, and let the woman be on her back, spread her legs.
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	Then join the two hands together, so that the small finger may run, and cover the nipples;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	Then take wool, and dip it in oil, and put it on the spot, and let the woman lie on her back every day, so that he cannot hold it in place.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the syrup is thick and heavy, you must take a spoon that resembles a leaf of thyme.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the nipple is erect, then hang it from a chain and cover it;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	And put the medicines which stop the blood, if as here, dragon's blood, incense, together with alumen;
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	Then put a wide patch of plaster on it, so that the wound cannot close;
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	And let it remain for a long time, and put a dry linen bandage on it;
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat with other remedies until it is well.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	When the mare gives birth to a foal, if she is covered in this way, there will be no abscesses.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For when the mare has an abscess that has formed, one must not touch her with fire.
des emorroides	hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Emorrhoids are openings of veins that, without proper care, and when the hemorrhoids become old, turn into thorns.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	And we have said in the division the appearances of ears, and signs, and I will say here those that yield cure.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and the hymen, when they are fully developed in the body, do not come to light except for the treatment by iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those who are at the mouth of the vagina can be felt, they can be cured.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	It is therefore necessary that you put the woman in a cold house, and let the thorns grow at the root, and powder on curative medicines that restrain blood, if possible and suitable, such as here is given and blood of dragon and incense, and similar things;
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	then pour water on the roots for an hour, then put her in cold water.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	and if the blood comes out, let her sit in a bath of sumac and bark of pomegranates and gall and similar things, and then take barley flour, and confound it with honey and water, and make an ointment therefrom which you apply to her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it stops, it's good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If so, make him feel no pain with ventosas on his back and at his breasts without hurting him;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	Then take another, and the juice of plantain or of nettle with old wine, and make him feel it at his place.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess is healed, keep the wound clean until it is well.
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	and that which is called “albatyr” is red, and has the appearance of a sharp knife, so cover it as I have said in the text;
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then the cure until he is well.
des apostemes de la marris	The abscesses of the breasts
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Various kinds of abscesses can appear in the breast, such as syphilis, painful abscesses, herpes, suppurations, fistulas, hemorrhoids, hot abscesses, and many other diseases which I have mentioned in the classification.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	It therefore follows that I should describe in this treatise the hot abscess which comes on the breast, which is not an abscess of putrefaction;
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	and if you want to know the work of iron, see if, when the abscess is beginning to come, it is hot and full of fever, and if it turns red, then you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Do not then hurry to pierce, but let it die as long as the pain is soothed.
